/README.md:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1 | 
  2 | # Connect: Commitment Management Application
  3 | 
  4 | ## About Connect
  5 | 
  6 | Connect is a modern web application designed to help users create, manage and track various types of commitments between parties. Whether personal promises, business agreements, or contracts, Connect provides a secure and transparent way to document and verify commitments.
  7 | 
  8 | ## Features
  9 | 
 10 | - User authentication and profile management
 11 | - Create and manage different types of commitments
 12 | - Real-time updates on commitment status
 13 | - Document storage for commitment-related files
 14 | - Connection management between users
 15 | - Digital wallet integration
 16 | 
 17 | ## Technical Stack
 18 | 
 19 | - **Frontend**: React, TypeScript, Tailwind CSS, shadcn/ui
 20 | - **Backend**: Supabase (PostgreSQL, Auth, Storage, Functions)
 21 | - **State Management**: TanStack Query (React Query)
 22 | - **Styling**: Tailwind CSS with custom theme
 23 | - **Authentication**: Supabase Auth
 24 | 
 25 | ## Getting Started
 26 | 
 27 | ### Prerequisites
 28 | 
 29 | - Node.js 18+ and npm
 30 | - Supabase account
 31 | 
 32 | ### Installation
 33 | 
 34 | 1. Clone the repository:
 35 | ```sh
 36 | git clone <repository-url>
 37 | cd connect
 38 | ```
 39 | 
 40 | 2. Install dependencies:
 41 | ```sh
 42 | npm install
 43 | ```
 44 | 
 45 | 3. Configure environment variables:
 46 | Create a `.env` file in the project root with the following variables:
 47 | ```
 48 | VITE_SUPABASE_URL=your_supabase_url
 49 | VITE_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY=your_supabase_anon_key
 50 | ```
 51 | 
 52 | 4. Run the development server:
 53 | ```sh
 54 | npm run dev
 55 | ```
 56 | 
 57 | ## Backend Architecture
 58 | 
 59 | The application uses Supabase as its backend with the potential to migrate to AWS QLDB in the future. For detailed information on the backend architecture, see:
 60 | 
 61 | - [Backend Architecture Documentation](./docs/BACKEND_ARCHITECTURE.md)
 62 | - [Supabase to QLDB Migration Guide](./docs/SUPABASE_TO_QLDB_MIGRATION.md)
 63 | 
 64 | ## Database Schema
 65 | 
 66 | The following tables are used in the Supabase database:
 67 | 
 68 | ### profiles
 69 | - Stores user profile information
 70 | - Automatically created when a user signs up
 71 | 
 72 | ### commitments
 73 | - Core table for commitment data
 74 | - Stores common fields like title, description, status
 75 | 
 76 | ### commitment_parties
 77 | - Junction table for users involved in commitments
 78 | - Defines the role of each user in the commitment
 79 | 
 80 | ### commitment_documents
 81 | - Stores document references for commitments
 82 | - Links to files in Storage
 83 | 
 84 | ### commitment_history
 85 | - Tracks changes to commitments over time
 86 | - Useful for audit and verification
 87 | 
 88 | ## API Documentation
 89 | 
 90 | The application uses Supabase as its backend API. The CommitmentService class provides methods for interacting with the Supabase API:
 91 | 
 92 | - `createCommitment`: Creates a new commitment
 93 | - `getUserCommitments`: Gets all commitments created by the current user
 94 | - `getParticipatingCommitments`: Gets all commitments where the user is a participant
 95 | - `getCommitmentById`: Gets a specific commitment by its ID
 96 | - `updateCommitment`: Updates a commitment's details
 97 | - `updateCommitmentStatus`: Updates a commitment's status
 98 | - `deleteCommitment`: Deletes a commitment
 99 | 
100 | ## Contributing
101 | 
102 | 1. Fork the repository
103 | 2. Create your feature branch (`git checkout -b feature/amazing-feature`)
104 | 3. Commit your changes (`git commit -m 'Add some amazing feature'`)
105 | 4. Push to the branch (`git push origin feature/amazing-feature`)
106 | 5. Open a Pull Request
107 | 
108 | ## License
109 | 
110 | This project is licensed under the MIT License - see the LICENSE file for details.
111 |

/docs/BACKEND_ARCHITECTURE.md:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1 | 
  2 | # Backend Architecture Documentation
  3 | 
  4 | ## Overview
  5 | 
  6 | This document outlines the backend architecture for the Connect application, which is designed to store and manage commitments between users. The system is initially implemented using Supabase for data storage but designed with the flexibility to migrate to Amazon QLDB (Quantum Ledger Database) in the future.
  7 | 
  8 | ## Core Components
  9 | 
 10 | ### 1. Data Storage Layer
 11 | 
 12 | #### Current Implementation: Supabase
 13 | 
 14 | The application uses Supabase as the primary data store with the following key features:
 15 | - **PostgreSQL Database**: Core relational database for storing all commitment and user data
 16 | - **Row-Level Security (RLS)**: Controls data access at the row level based on user authentication
 17 | - **Real-time Subscriptions**: Enables real-time updates to connected clients
 18 | 
 19 | #### Future Implementation: Amazon QLDB
 20 | 
 21 | Amazon QLDB provides:
 22 | - **Immutability**: Complete, cryptographically verifiable history of data changes
 23 | - **Blockchain-like Features**: Cryptographic verification without the distributed consensus overhead
 24 | - **Document-oriented Model**: Flexible schema for commitment data
 25 | 
 26 | ### 2. Authentication System
 27 | 
 28 | - **User Authentication**: Email/password, social logins, and token-based auth using Supabase Auth
 29 | - **Session Management**: Secure token handling and refresh mechanisms
 30 | - **Authorization**: Role-based access control for different commitment types
 31 | 
 32 | ### 3. API Layer
 33 | 
 34 | - **RESTful API**: For standard CRUD operations on commitments and user data
 35 | - **GraphQL API**: For more complex queries and real-time subscriptions
 36 | - **Serverless Functions**: For handling business logic, validations, and integrations
 37 | 
 38 | ### 4. Business Logic Layer
 39 | 
 40 | - **Commitment Management**: Creation, updates, status changes
 41 | - **Validation Service**: Ensures commitments meet required criteria
 42 | - **Notification System**: Alerts for commitment changes and deadlines
 43 | 
 44 | ## Database Schema
 45 | 
 46 | ### Key Tables
 47 | 
 48 | 1. **profiles**
 49 |    - User profile information linked to auth system
 50 | 
 51 | 2. **commitments**
 52 |    - Core table for all commitment records
 53 |    - Contains common fields like title, description, status
 54 |    - Linked to specific users via foreign keys
 55 | 
 56 | 3. **commitment_types**
 57 |    - Different types of commitments (personal, business, etc.)
 58 |    - Configuration for type-specific behavior
 59 | 
 60 | 4. **commitment_parties**
 61 |    - Junction table for many-to-many relationship between users and commitments
 62 |    - Stores the role of each user in the commitment (creator, participant, witness)
 63 | 
 64 | 5. **commitment_documents**
 65 |    - Stores links to documents associated with commitments
 66 |    - Handles document versioning and metadata
 67 | 
 68 | 6. **commitment_history**
 69 |    - Audit trail of all changes to commitments
 70 |    - Critical for verification and dispute resolution
 71 | 
 72 | ## Security Model
 73 | 
 74 | - **Row-Level Security**: Users can only access commitments they're authorized to see
 75 | - **Data Encryption**: Sensitive data fields are encrypted at rest
 76 | - **API Authentication**: JWT-based authentication for all API requests
 77 | - **Input Validation**: Thorough validation of all user inputs
 78 | 
 79 | ## Migration Path: Supabase to QLDB
 80 | 
 81 | ### Phase 1: Supabase Implementation
 82 | - Implement core functionality using Supabase
 83 | - Design schema with future migration in mind
 84 | 
 85 | ### Phase 2: Hybrid Operation
 86 | - Implement QLDB connectors alongside existing Supabase system
 87 | - Begin dual-writing critical commitment data to both systems
 88 | - Implement verification processes between systems
 89 | 
 90 | ### Phase 3: Full Migration
 91 | - Migrate historical data from Supabase to QLDB
 92 | - Update all read operations to use QLDB as source of truth
 93 | - Decommission Supabase components once migration is verified
 94 | 
 95 | ## Integration Points
 96 | 
 97 | - **Payment Processing**: Integration with payment gateways for financial commitments
 98 | - **Calendar Systems**: For deadline management and reminders
 99 | - **Document Storage**: For storing and managing commitment-related documents
100 | - **Notification Services**: Email, SMS, and push notifications for important events
101 | 
102 | ## Monitoring and Operations
103 | 
104 | - **Logging Strategy**: Structured logging with different verbosity levels
105 | - **Metrics Collection**: Performance metrics for all key components
106 | - **Alerting System**: Proactive alerts for potential issues
107 | - **Backup Strategy**: Regular backups with point-in-time recovery
108 | 
109 | ## Technical Requirements
110 | 
111 | - **Scalability**: Designed to handle thousands of concurrent users
112 | - **Availability**: 99.9% uptime target
113 | - **Performance**: API response times under 200ms for standard operations
114 | - **Data Integrity**: Cryptographic verification of all commitment data
115 | 


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/docs/SUPABASE_TO_QLDB_MIGRATION.md:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1 | 
  2 | # Migration Guide: From Supabase to Amazon QLDB
  3 | 
  4 | This document outlines the process for migrating from Supabase to Amazon QLDB (Quantum Ledger Database) for the Connect application's commitment storage system.
  5 | 
  6 | ## Why Migrate to QLDB?
  7 | 
  8 | While Supabase provides an excellent starting point with its PostgreSQL database, auth system, and real-time capabilities, Amazon QLDB offers specific advantages for commitment tracking:
  9 | 
 10 | 1. **Immutable History**: QLDB maintains a complete, immutable, and cryptographically verifiable history of all data changes.
 11 | 2. **Built-in Verification**: Cryptographic verification of data integrity without the overhead of a distributed consensus mechanism.
 12 | 3. **Audit Trail**: Complete audit trail for regulatory compliance and dispute resolution.
 13 | 4. **Performance**: High transaction throughput with consistent, predictable performance.
 14 | 
 15 | ## Migration Strategy
 16 | 
 17 | ### 1. Preparation Phase
 18 | 
 19 | #### Data Mapping
 20 | - Map Supabase table structures to QLDB document structures
 21 | - Design the QLDB ledger and table organization
 22 | - Create data transformation scripts for the migration
 23 | 
 24 | #### API Abstraction
 25 | - Implement a data access abstraction layer if not already present
 26 | - This allows switching between Supabase and QLDB without changing application code
 27 | 
 28 | #### Testing Environment
 29 | - Set up a parallel QLDB environment for testing
 30 | - Create test datasets representative of production data
 31 | 
 32 | ### 2. Implementation Phase
 33 | 
 34 | #### QLDB Setup
 35 | ```typescript
 36 | // Example QLDB setup code
 37 | import { QldbDriver, RetryConfig } from 'amazon-qldb-driver-nodejs';
 38 | 
 39 | const maxRetries = 3;
 40 | const retryConfig = new RetryConfig(maxRetries);
 41 | 
 42 | const qldbDriver = new QldbDriver('connect-commitments-ledger', 
 43 |   { retryConfig });
 44 | 
 45 | // Create tables and indexes
 46 | await qldbDriver.executeLambda(async (txn) => {
 47 |   await txn.execute('CREATE TABLE commitments');
 48 |   await txn.execute('CREATE INDEX ON commitments (id)');
 49 |   await txn.execute('CREATE INDEX ON commitments (createdBy)');
 50 |   // Additional tables and indexes as needed
 51 | });
 52 | ```
 53 | 
 54 | #### Data Access Layer
 55 | ```typescript
 56 | // Example data access layer
 57 | class CommitmentRepository {
 58 |   // Interface methods
 59 |   async getCommitmentById(id: string): Promise<Commitment> {
 60 |     // Implementation will vary based on current storage
 61 |     if (useQldb) {
 62 |       return this.getCommitmentFromQldb(id);
 63 |     } else {
 64 |       return this.getCommitmentFromSupabase(id);
 65 |     }
 66 |   }
 67 |   
 68 |   // Supabase implementation
 69 |   private async getCommitmentFromSupabase(id: string): Promise<Commitment> {
 70 |     const { data, error } = await supabase
 71 |       .from('commitments')
 72 |       .select('*')
 73 |       .eq('id', id)
 74 |       .single();
 75 |       
 76 |     if (error) throw error;
 77 |     return data;
 78 |   }
 79 |   
 80 |   // QLDB implementation
 81 |   private async getCommitmentFromQldb(id: string): Promise<Commitment> {
 82 |     const result = await qldbDriver.executeLambda(async (txn) => {
 83 |       return await txn.execute(
 84 |         'SELECT * FROM commitments WHERE id = ?', id
 85 |       );
 86 |     });
 87 |     
 88 |     if (result.getResultList().length === 0) {
 89 |       throw new Error('Commitment not found');
 90 |     }
 91 |     
 92 |     return result.getResultList()[0].toJSON() as Commitment;
 93 |   }
 94 | }
 95 | ```
 96 | 
 97 | ### 3. Migration Phase
 98 | 
 99 | #### Dual-Write Stage
100 | - Update application to write to both Supabase and QLDB
101 | - Continue reading from Supabase as the source of truth
102 | - Implement verification routines to ensure data consistency
103 | 
104 | #### Data Migration
105 | - Export existing data from Supabase
106 | - Transform data to fit QLDB document model
107 | - Import data into QLDB with appropriate timestamps and metadata
108 | 
109 | #### Cutover Stage
110 | - Update application to read from QLDB
111 | - Monitor for any issues during a controlled rollout
112 | - Maintain Supabase as a fallback for a defined grace period
113 | 
114 | ### 4. Post-Migration Phase
115 | 
116 | #### Verification
117 | - Run comprehensive data integrity checks
118 | - Ensure all application features work correctly with QLDB
119 | - Validate performance meets requirements
120 | 
121 | #### Cleanup
122 | - Decommission Supabase components once QLDB is stable
123 | - Remove dual-write code paths
124 | - Archive Supabase data for reference
125 | 
126 | ## QLDB Specific Considerations
127 | 
128 | ### Document Model
129 | QLDB uses a document data model similar to MongoDB rather than the relational model of PostgreSQL. Design your documents to take advantage of this:
130 | 
131 | ```json
132 | {
133 |   "id": "commit-123",
134 |   "title": "Business Partnership Agreement",
135 |   "description": "Terms for partnership between Company A and Company B",
136 |   "type": "business",
137 |   "status": "active",
138 |   "createdAt": "2023-04-01T12:00:00Z",
139 |   "createdBy": "user-456",
140 |   "parties": [
141 |     {
142 |       "userId": "user-456",
143 |       "role": "creator"
144 |     },
145 |     {
146 |       "userId": "user-789",
147 |       "role": "participant"
148 |     }
149 |   ],
150 |   "terms": "Both parties agree to share profits equally...",
151 |   "documents": [
152 |     {
153 |       "name": "contract.pdf",
154 |       "url": "https://storage.example.com/contract.pdf",
155 |       "uploadedAt": "2023-04-01T12:05:00Z"
156 |     }
157 |   ]
158 | }
159 | ```
160 | 
161 | ### Historical Queries
162 | QLDB excels at historical queries using its built-in history function:
163 | 
164 | ```sql
165 | SELECT h.data.title, h.metadata.version 
166 | FROM history(commitments) AS h 
167 | WHERE h.data.id = 'commit-123'
168 | ```
169 | 
170 | ### Verification
171 | Use QLDB's digest functionality to verify the integrity of your data:
172 | 
173 | ```typescript
174 | async function verifyCommitment(commitmentId: string, expectedDigest: string): Promise<boolean> {
175 |   const digest = await qldbDriver.getDigest();
176 |   
177 |   const proof = await qldbDriver.getRevision({
178 |     blockAddress: {
179 |       strandId: "00000001",
180 |       sequenceNo: 123
181 |     },
182 |     documentId: commitmentId,
183 |     digestTipAddress: digest.digestTipAddress
184 |   });
185 |   
186 |   return QLDB.verifyDocument({
187 |     documentHash: proof.proof.hash,
188 |     digest: proof.digest,
189 |     proof: proof.proof
190 |   });
191 | }
192 | ```
193 | 
194 | ## Technical Challenges
195 | 
196 | ### Data Consistency
197 | - Ensure all QLDB transactions are ACID compliant
198 | - Handle conflict resolution during the dual-write phase
199 | 
200 | ### Schema Differences
201 | - Address differences between relational and document models
202 | - Optimize document structure for common query patterns
203 | 
204 | ### Performance Tuning
205 | - Adjust QLDB read/write capacity for optimal performance
206 | - Implement appropriate caching strategies
207 | 
208 | ## Rollback Plan
209 | 
210 | In case of critical issues during migration:
211 | 1. Revert application to read from Supabase
212 | 2. Continue dual-writing to both systems
213 | 3. Address issues in the QLDB implementation
214 | 4. Retry migration after resolving problems
215 | 
216 | ## Timeline and Resources
217 | 
218 | - **Planning**: 2-3 weeks
219 | - **Implementation**: 4-6 weeks
220 | - **Migration**: 1-2 weeks
221 | - **Validation and Cleanup**: 2 weeks
222 | 
223 | **Required Resources**:
224 | - Backend developers familiar with both Supabase and AWS
225 | - DevOps engineer for AWS infrastructure setup
226 | - QA resources for thorough testing
227 | - Product owner involvement for feature validation
228 |

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/src/App.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | 
 2 | import { Toaster } from "@/components/ui/toaster";
 3 | import { Toaster as Sonner } from "@/components/ui/sonner";
 4 | import { TooltipProvider } from "@/components/ui/tooltip";
 5 | import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from "@tanstack/react-query";
 6 | import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route } from "react-router-dom";
 7 | import { AuthProvider } from "@/contexts/AuthContext";
 8 | import ProtectedRoute from "@/components/auth/ProtectedRoute";
 9 | import AuthCallback from "@/components/auth/AuthCallback";
10 | import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
11 | import { ThemeProvider } from "@/contexts/ThemeContext";
12 | import Index from "./pages/Index";
13 | import Login from "./pages/Login";
14 | import Register from "./pages/Register";
15 | import Dashboard from "./pages/Dashboard";
16 | import Connections from "./pages/Connections";
17 | import Wallet from "./pages/Wallet";
18 | import Profile from "./pages/Profile";
19 | import NotFound from "./pages/NotFound";
20 | import { StrictMode } from "react";
21 | import CreateCommitment from "./pages/CreateCommitment";
22 | import CommitmentDetails from "./pages/CommitmentDetails";
23 | 
24 | const queryClient = new QueryClient({
25 |   defaultOptions: {
26 |     queries: {
27 |       refetchOnWindowFocus: false,
28 |       staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000, // 5 minutes
29 |     }
30 |   }
31 | });
32 | 
33 | const PageTransition = ({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) => {
34 |   return (
35 |     <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
36 |       <motion.div
37 |         initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
38 |         animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
39 |         exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
40 |         transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
41 |       >
42 |         {children}
43 |       </motion.div>
44 |     </AnimatePresence>
45 |   );
46 | };
47 | 
48 | const App = () => (
49 |   <StrictMode>
50 |     <ThemeProvider>
51 |       <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
52 |         <BrowserRouter>
53 |           <AuthProvider>
54 |             <TooltipProvider>
55 |               <Toaster />
56 |               <Sonner />
57 |               <Routes>
58 |                 {/* Public routes */}
59 |                 <Route path="/" element={<PageTransition><Index /></PageTransition>} />
60 |                 <Route path="/login" element={<PageTransition><Login /></PageTransition>} />
61 |                 <Route path="/register" element={<PageTransition><Register /></PageTransition>} />
62 |                 <Route path="/auth/callback" element={<AuthCallback />} />
63 |                 
64 |                 {/* Protected routes */}
65 |                 <Route element={<ProtectedRoute />}>
66 |                   <Route path="/dashboard" element={<PageTransition><Dashboard /></PageTransition>} />
67 |                   <Route path="/connections" element={<PageTransition><Connections /></PageTransition>} />
68 |                   <Route path="/wallet" element={<PageTransition><Wallet /></PageTransition>} />
69 |                   <Route path="/profile" element={<PageTransition><Profile /></PageTransition>} />
70 |                   <Route path="/create-commitment" element={<PageTransition><CreateCommitment /></PageTransition>} />
71 |                   <Route path="/commitment/:id" element={<PageTransition><CommitmentDetails /></PageTransition>} />
72 |                 </Route>
73 |                 
74 |                 {/* 404 route */}
75 |                 <Route path="*" element={<PageTransition><NotFound /></PageTransition>} />
76 |               </Routes>
77 |             </TooltipProvider>
78 |           </AuthProvider>
79 |         </BrowserRouter>
80 |       </QueryClientProvider>
81 |     </ThemeProvider>
82 |   </StrictMode>
83 | );
84 | 
85 | export default App;
86 |

/src/components/CommitmentCard.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1 | 
  2 | import { Link } from "react-router-dom";
  3 | import { Card, CardHeader, CardContent, CardFooter } from "./ui/card";
  4 | import { Badge } from "./ui/badge";
  5 | import { CommitmentType } from "@/types/commitments";
  6 | import { User, Briefcase, FileText, BookOpen, Handshake, Heart, Lock, Calendar, Clock, Users } from "lucide-react";
  7 | import { motion } from "framer-motion";
  8 | 
  9 | export interface CommitmentProps {
 10 |   id: string;
 11 |   title: string;
 12 |   description: string;
 13 |   parties: string[];
 14 |   deadline?: string;
 15 |   status: "active" | "pending" | "completed" | "expired";
 16 |   createdAt: string;
 17 |   value?: number;
 18 |   type?: CommitmentType;
 19 | }
 20 | 
 21 | const CommitmentCard = ({
 22 |   id,
 23 |   title,
 24 |   description,
 25 |   parties,
 26 |   deadline,
 27 |   status,
 28 |   createdAt,
 29 |   value,
 30 |   type = "personal",
 31 | }: CommitmentProps) => {
 32 |   const getStatusColor = (status: string) => {
 33 |     switch (status) {
 34 |       case "active":
 35 |         return "bg-green-100 text-green-800 dark:bg-green-900/30 dark:text-green-300";
 36 |       case "pending":
 37 |         return "bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800 dark:bg-yellow-900/30 dark:text-yellow-300";
 38 |       case "completed":
 39 |         return "bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 dark:bg-blue-900/30 dark:text-blue-300";
 40 |       case "expired":
 41 |         return "bg-red-100 text-red-800 dark:bg-red-900/30 dark:text-red-300";
 42 |       default:
 43 |         return "bg-gray-100 text-gray-800 dark:bg-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300";
 44 |     }
 45 |   };
 46 | 
 47 |   const getTypeIcon = () => {
 48 |     switch (type) {
 49 |       case "personal":
 50 |         return <User className="h-5 w-5" />;
 51 |       case "business":
 52 |         return <Briefcase className="h-5 w-5" />;
 53 |       case "contract":
 54 |         return <FileText className="h-5 w-5" />;
 55 |       case "religious":
 56 |         return <BookOpen className="h-5 w-5" />;
 57 |       case "promise":
 58 |         return <Handshake className="h-5 w-5" />;
 59 |       case "friendly":
 60 |         return <Heart className="h-5 w-5" />;
 61 |       case "trust":
 62 |         return <Lock className="h-5 w-5" />;
 63 |       default:
 64 |         return <User className="h-5 w-5" />;
 65 |     }
 66 |   };
 67 | 
 68 |   const getTypeColor = () => {
 69 |     switch (type) {
 70 |       case "personal":
 71 |         return "bg-blue-100 text-blue-600 dark:bg-blue-900/30 dark:text-blue-400";
 72 |       case "business":
 73 |         return "bg-purple-100 text-purple-600 dark:bg-purple-900/30 dark:text-purple-400";
 74 |       case "contract":
 75 |         return "bg-gray-100 text-gray-600 dark:bg-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300";
 76 |       case "religious":
 77 |         return "bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-600 dark:bg-yellow-900/30 dark:text-yellow-400";
 78 |       case "promise":
 79 |         return "bg-green-100 text-green-600 dark:bg-green-900/30 dark:text-green-400";
 80 |       case "friendly":
 81 |         return "bg-pink-100 text-pink-600 dark:bg-pink-900/30 dark:text-pink-400";
 82 |       case "trust":
 83 |         return "bg-red-100 text-red-600 dark:bg-red-900/30 dark:text-red-400";
 84 |       default:
 85 |         return "bg-blue-100 text-blue-600 dark:bg-blue-900/30 dark:text-blue-400";
 86 |     }
 87 |   };
 88 | 
 89 |   return (
 90 |     <motion.div 
 91 |       whileHover={{ scale: 1.02, y: -5 }}
 92 |       transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300 }}
 93 |     >
 94 |       <Link to={`/commitment/${id}`}>
 95 |         <Card className="h-full overflow-hidden shadow-sm hover:shadow-lg transition-shadow duration-300">
 96 |           <CardHeader className="pb-3 pt-4">
 97 |             <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
 98 |               <div className="flex items-center space-x-3">
 99 |                 <div className={`p-2 rounded-full ${getTypeColor()}`}>
100 |                   {getTypeIcon()}
101 |                 </div>
102 |                 <div>
103 |                   <h3 className="font-semibold leading-tight">{title}</h3>
104 |                   <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 capitalize">{type}</p>
105 |                 </div>
106 |               </div>
107 |               <Badge className={getStatusColor(status)}>
108 |                 {status.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + status.slice(1)}
109 |               </Badge>
110 |             </div>
111 |           </CardHeader>
112 |           <CardContent className="pb-3">
113 |             <p className="text-sm line-clamp-2 text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300 mb-4">
114 |               {description}
115 |             </p>
116 |             
117 |             <div className="space-y-2">
118 |               <div className="flex items-center text-sm text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">
119 |                 <Users className="h-3.5 w-3.5 mr-1.5" />
120 |                 <span className="line-clamp-1">
121 |                   {parties.join(", ")}
122 |                 </span>
123 |               </div>
124 |               
125 |               {deadline && (
126 |                 <div className="flex items-center text-sm text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">
127 |                   <Calendar className="h-3.5 w-3.5 mr-1.5" />
128 |                   <span>Due: {new Date(deadline).toLocaleDateString()}</span>
129 |                 </div>
130 |               )}
131 |               
132 |               {value && (
133 |                 <div className="flex items-center text-sm font-medium">
134 |                   <span className="text-primary dark:text-primary/90">${value.toLocaleString()}</span>
135 |                 </div>
136 |               )}
137 |             </div>
138 |           </CardContent>
139 |           <CardFooter className="pt-0 pb-4 text-xs text-gray-400 dark:text-gray-500">
140 |             <div className="flex items-center">
141 |               <Clock className="h-3 w-3 mr-1" />
142 |               Created {new Date(createdAt).toLocaleDateString()}
143 |             </div>
144 |           </CardFooter>
145 |         </Card>
146 |       </Link>
147 |     </motion.div>
148 |   );
149 | };
150 | 
151 | export default CommitmentCard;
152 |

 73 |             </button>
 74 |           </div>
 75 |         </div>

100 |                 onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)}

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/src/components/auth/AuthCallback.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | 
 2 | import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
 3 | import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
 4 | import { supabase } from "@/integrations/supabase/client";
 5 | import { Loader2 } from "lucide-react";
 6 | 
 7 | const AuthCallback = () => {
 8 |   const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
 9 |   const navigate = useNavigate();
10 | 
11 |   useEffect(() => {
12 |     const handleAuthCallback = async () => {
13 |       try {
14 |         const { error } = await supabase.auth.getSession();
15 |         if (error) throw error;
16 |         
17 |         // If session creation was successful, navigate to dashboard
18 |         navigate("/dashboard");
19 |       } catch (err: any) {
20 |         setError(err.message);
21 |         // If there was an error, navigate back to the login page
22 |         setTimeout(() => {
23 |           navigate("/login");
24 |         }, 3000);
25 |       }
26 |     };
27 | 
28 |     handleAuthCallback();
29 |   }, [navigate]);
30 | 
31 |   if (error) {
32 |     return (
33 |       <div className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center">
34 |         <div className="text-center">
35 |           <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-red-500">Authentication Error</h2>
36 |           <p className="mt-2">{error}</p>
37 |           <p className="mt-4">Redirecting to login page...</p>
38 |         </div>
39 |       </div>
40 |     );
41 |   }
42 | 
43 |   return (
44 |     <div className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center">
45 |       <div className="text-center">
46 |         <Loader2 className="mx-auto h-12 w-12 animate-spin text-connect-500" />
47 |         <h2 className="mt-4 text-xl font-medium">Finalizing authentication...</h2>
48 |         <p className="mt-2 text-gray-500">Please wait while we complete the sign in process.</p>
49 |       </div>
50 |     </div>
51 |   );
52 | };
53 | 
54 | export default AuthCallback;
55 | 


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/src/components/auth/EmailLoginForm.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | 
 2 | import { useState } from "react";
 3 | import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
 4 | import { Link } from "react-router-dom";
 5 | import { Mail, Lock, Loader2 } from "lucide-react";
 6 | import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
 7 | import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
 8 | import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
 9 | import { useAuth } from "@/contexts/AuthContext";
10 | 
11 | interface EmailLoginFormProps {
12 |   onError: (message: string) => void;
13 | }
14 | 
15 | const EmailLoginForm = ({ onError }: EmailLoginFormProps) => {
16 |   const [email, setEmail] = useState("");
17 |   const [password, setPassword] = useState("");
18 |   const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
19 |   
20 |   const { signIn } = useAuth();
21 |   const navigate = useNavigate();
22 | 
23 |   const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
24 |     e.preventDefault();
25 |     setIsLoading(true);
26 |     
27 |     try {
28 |       await signIn(email, password);
29 |       navigate("/dashboard");
30 |     } catch (error: any) {
31 |       console.error("Login error:", error);
32 |       if (error.message?.includes("Invalid login credentials")) {
33 |         onError("Invalid email or password. Please check your credentials and try again.");
34 |       } else {
35 |         onError(error.message || "An error occurred during login");
36 |       }
37 |     } finally {
38 |       setIsLoading(false);
39 |     }
40 |   };
41 | 
42 |   return (
43 |     <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
44 |       <div className="space-y-2">
45 |         <Label htmlFor="email">Email</Label>
46 |         <div className="relative">
47 |           <Mail className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 h-4 w-4 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-500" />
48 |           <Input 
49 |             id="email" 
50 |             type="email" 
51 |             placeholder="name@example.com" 
52 |             value={email}
53 |             onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
54 |             className="pl-10"
55 |             required
56 |           />
57 |         </div>
58 |       </div>
59 |       <div className="space-y-2">
60 |         <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
61 |           <Label htmlFor="password">Password</Label>
62 |           <Link to="/forgot-password" className="text-sm text-connect-500 hover:text-connect-600">
63 |             Forgot password?
64 |           </Link>
65 |         </div>
66 |         <div className="relative">
67 |           <Lock className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 h-4 w-4 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-500" />
68 |           <Input 
69 |             id="password" 
70 |             type="password" 
71 |             placeholder="••••••••" 
72 |             value={password}
73 |             onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
74 |             className="pl-10"
75 |             required
76 |           />
77 |         </div>
78 |       </div>
79 |       <Button 
80 |         type="submit" 
81 |         className="w-full bg-connect-500 hover:bg-connect-600"
82 |         disabled={isLoading}
83 |       >
84 |         {isLoading ? (
85 |           <>
86 |             <Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />
87 |             Signing In...
88 |           </>
89 |         ) : (
90 |           "Sign In"
91 |         )}
92 |       </Button>
93 |     </form>
94 |   );
95 | };
96 | 
97 | export default EmailLoginForm;
98 |

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/src/components/auth/PhoneLoginForm.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | 
 2 | import { useState } from "react";
 3 | import { Phone } from "lucide-react";
 4 | import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
 5 | import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
 6 | import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
 7 | import { toast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
 8 | 
 9 | const PhoneLoginForm = () => {
10 |   const [phone, setPhone] = useState("");
11 |   const [otp, setOtp] = useState("");
12 |   const [isOtpSent, setIsOtpSent] = useState(false);
13 | 
14 |   const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
15 |     e.preventDefault();
16 |     if (isOtpSent) {
17 |       toast({
18 |         title: "Feature not implemented",
19 |         description: "Phone verification is not yet implemented",
20 |       });
21 |     } else {
22 |       toast({
23 |         title: "Feature not implemented",
24 |         description: "Phone verification is not yet implemented",
25 |       });
26 |       // For demo purposes, we'll simulate OTP being sent
27 |       setIsOtpSent(true);
28 |     }
29 |   };
30 | 
31 |   return (
32 |     <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
33 |       <div className="space-y-2">
34 |         <Label htmlFor="phone">Phone Number</Label>
35 |         <div className="relative">
36 |           <Phone className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 h-4 w-4 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-500" />
37 |           <Input 
38 |             id="phone" 
39 |             type="tel" 
40 |             placeholder="+1 (555) 000-0000" 
41 |             value={phone}
42 |             onChange={(e) => setPhone(e.target.value)}
43 |             className="pl-10"
44 |             required
45 |             disabled={isOtpSent}
46 |           />
47 |         </div>
48 |       </div>
49 |       
50 |       {isOtpSent && (
51 |         <div className="space-y-2">
52 |           <Label htmlFor="otp">Verification Code</Label>
53 |           <Input 
54 |             id="otp" 
55 |             type="text" 
56 |             placeholder="Enter 6-digit code" 
57 |             value={otp}
58 |             onChange={(e) => setOtp(e.target.value)}
59 |             maxLength={6}
60 |             required
61 |           />
62 |         </div>
63 |       )}
64 |       
65 |       <Button type="submit" className="w-full bg-connect-500 hover:bg-connect-600">
66 |         {isOtpSent ? "Verify Code" : "Send Verification Code"}
67 |       </Button>
68 |       
69 |       {isOtpSent && (
70 |         <Button 
71 |           type="button" 
72 |           variant="outline" 
73 |           onClick={() => setIsOtpSent(false)} 
74 |           className="w-full mt-2"
75 |         >
76 |           Change Phone Number
77 |         </Button>
78 |       )}
79 |     </form>
80 |   );
81 | };
82 | 
83 | export default PhoneLoginForm;

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/src/components/auth/ProtectedRoute.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | 
 2 | import { Navigate, Outlet, useLocation } from "react-router-dom";
 3 | import { useAuth } from "@/contexts/AuthContext";
 4 | import { Loader2 } from "lucide-react";
 5 | 
 6 | const ProtectedRoute = () => {
 7 |   const { user, isLoading } = useAuth();
 8 |   const location = useLocation();
 9 | 
10 |   if (isLoading) {
11 |     return (
12 |       <div className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center">
13 |         <Loader2 className="h-8 w-8 animate-spin text-connect-500" />
14 |       </div>
15 |     );
16 |   }
17 | 
18 |   if (!user) {
19 |     // Redirect to login but save the location they were trying to access
20 |     return <Navigate to="/login" state={{ from: location }} replace />;
21 |   }
22 | 
23 |   // If authenticated, render the child routes
24 |   return <Outlet />;
25 | };
26 | 
27 | export default ProtectedRoute;
28 |

/src/components/auth/RegisterForm.tsx:

  1 | 
  2 | import { useState } from "react";
  3 | import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
  4 | import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
  5 | import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
  6 | import { Card, CardContent, CardDescription, CardFooter, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";
  7 | import { Mail, Lock, User, Facebook, Twitter, Linkedin } from "lucide-react";
  8 | import { Link, useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
  9 | import { useAuth } from "@/contexts/AuthContext";
 10 | import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
 11 | 
 12 | const RegisterForm = () => {
 13 |   const [firstName, setFirstName] = useState("");
 14 |   const [lastName, setLastName] = useState("");
 15 |   const [email, setEmail] = useState("");
 16 |   const [password, setPassword] = useState("");
 17 |   const [confirmPassword, setConfirmPassword] = useState("");
 18 |   const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
 19 |   
 20 |   const { signUp, signInWithProvider } = useAuth();
 21 |   const { toast } = useToast();
 22 |   const navigate = useNavigate();
 23 | 
 24 |   const handleRegister = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
 25 |     e.preventDefault();
 26 |     
 27 |     if (password !== confirmPassword) {
 28 |       toast({
 29 |         title: "Passwords don't match",
 30 |         description: "Please ensure both passwords are the same",
 31 |         variant: "destructive",
 32 |       });
 33 |       return;
 34 |     }
 35 |     
 36 |     setIsLoading(true);
 37 |     
 38 |     try {
 39 |       await signUp(email, password, {
 40 |         full_name: `${firstName} ${lastName}`,
 41 |         username: email.split('@')[0], // Default username from email
 42 |       });
 43 |       
 44 |       // In a real app, we might show a verification needed screen
 45 |       navigate("/login");
 46 |     } catch (error) {
 47 |       console.error("Registration error:", error);
 48 |     } finally {
 49 |       setIsLoading(false);
 50 |     }
 51 |   };
 52 | 
 53 |   const handleSocialLogin = async (provider: "facebook" | "twitter" | "linkedin") => {
 54 |     try {
 55 |       await signInWithProvider(provider);
 56 |     } catch (error) {
 57 |       console.error(`${provider} login error:`, error);
 58 |     }
 59 |   };
 60 | 
 61 |   return (
 62 |     <Card className="w-full max-w-md mx-auto">
 63 |       <CardHeader className="space-y-1">
 64 |         <CardTitle className="text-2xl text-center">Create an account</CardTitle>
 65 |         <CardDescription className="text-center">
 66 |           Enter your information to create a Connect account
 67 |         </CardDescription>
 68 |       </CardHeader>
 69 |       <CardContent>
 70 |         <form onSubmit={handleRegister} className="space-y-4">
 71 |           <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
 72 |             <div className="space-y-2">
 73 |               <Label htmlFor="firstName">First Name</Label>
 74 |               <div className="relative">
 75 |                 <User className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 h-4 w-4 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-500" />
 76 |                 <Input 
 77 |                   id="firstName" 
 78 |                   placeholder="John" 
 79 |                   value={firstName}
 80 |                   onChange={(e) => setFirstName(e.target.value)}
 81 |                   className="pl-10"
 82 |                   required
 83 |                 />
 84 |               </div>
 85 |             </div>
 86 |             <div className="space-y-2">
 87 |               <Label htmlFor="lastName">Last Name</Label>
 88 |               <Input 
 89 |                 id="lastName" 
 90 |                 placeholder="Doe" 
 91 |                 value={lastName}
 92 |                 onChange={(e) => setLastName(e.target.value)}
 93 |                 required
 94 |               />
 95 |             </div>
 96 |           </div>
 97 |           
 98 |           <div className="space-y-2">
 99 |             <Label htmlFor="email">Email</Label>
100 |             <div className="relative">
101 |               <Mail className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 h-4 w-4 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-500" />
102 |               <Input 
103 |                 id="email" 
104 |                 type="email" 
105 |                 placeholder="name@example.com" 
106 |                 value={email}
107 |                 onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
108 |                 className="pl-10"
109 |                 required
110 |               />
111 |             </div>
112 |           </div>
113 |           
114 |           <div className="space-y-2">
115 |             <Label htmlFor="password">Password</Label>
116 |             <div className="relative">
117 |               <Lock className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 h-4 w-4 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-500" />
118 |               <Input 
119 |                 id="password" 
120 |                 type="password" 
121 |                 placeholder="••••••••" 
122 |                 value={password}
123 |                 onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
124 |                 className="pl-10"
125 |                 required
126 |               />
127 |             </div>
128 |           </div>
129 |           
130 |           <div className="space-y-2">
131 |             <Label htmlFor="confirmPassword">Confirm Password</Label>
132 |             <Input 
133 |               id="confirmPassword" 
134 |               type="password" 
135 |               placeholder="••••••••" 
136 |               value={confirmPassword}
137 |               onChange={(e) => setConfirmPassword(e.target.value)}
138 |               required
139 |             />
140 |           </div>
141 |           
142 |           <div className="text-xs text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">
143 |             By creating an account, you agree to our{" "}
144 |             <Link to="/terms" className="text-connect-500 hover:text-connect-600">
145 |               Terms of Service
146 |             </Link>{" "}
147 |             and{" "}

 8 | }
 9 | 
10 | const SocialLoginButtons = ({ onError }: SocialLoginButtonsProps) => {

12 | 
13 |   const handleSocialLogin = async (provider: "facebook" | "twitter" | "linkedin") => {
14 |     try {
15 |       await signInWithProvider(provider);
16 |       // Navigation will be handled by the callback component
17 |     } catch (error: any) {
18 |       console.error(`${provider} login error:`, error);
19 |       onError(`Error signing in with ${provider}: ${error.message}`);
20 |     }
21 |   };
22 | 
23 |   return (
24 |     <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3">
25 |       <Button 
26 |         type="button" 
27 |         variant="outline"

31 |         <Facebook className="h-4 w-4" />
32 |       </Button>

37 |         className="w-full"

39 |         <Twitter className="h-4 w-4" />
40 |       </Button>
41 |       <Button 
42 |         type="button"

45 |         className="w-full"
46 |       >
47 |         <Linkedin className="h-4 w-4" />

  6 | import { BusinessCommitment, TaggedUser } from "@/types/commitments";

 23 | 
 24 | const formSchema = z.object({
 25 |   title: z.string().min(3, "Title must be at least 3 characters"),
 26 |   description: z.string().min(10, "Description must be at least 10 characters"),
 27 |   terms: z.string().optional(),
 28 |   deadline: z.date().optional(),
 29 |   value: z.string().optional().transform(val => val ? parseFloat(val) : undefined)
 30 | });

 36 | const BusinessCommitmentForm = ({ onSubmit }: BusinessCommitmentFormProps) => {

 39 |   
 40 |   const form = useForm<z.infer<typeof formSchema>>({
 41 |     resolver: zodResolver(formSchema),
 42 |     defaultValues: {
 43 |       title: "",
 44 |       description: "",
 45 |       terms: "",
 46 |     }
 47 |   });
 48 |   
 49 |   const handleSubmit = (values: z.infer<typeof formSchema>) => {
 50 |     const commitmentData: Partial<BusinessCommitment> = {
 51 |       ...values,
 52 |       type: "business",
 53 |       parties,
 54 |       documents,
 55 |       deadline: values.deadline ? format(values.deadline, "yyyy-MM-dd") : undefined
 56 |     };
 57 |     
 58 |     onSubmit(commitmentData);
 59 |   };
 60 |   
 61 |   // Mock function for document upload
 62 |   const handleDocumentUpload = () => {
 63 |     const mockDocument = {
 64 |       name: `Document-${documents.length + 1}.pdf`,
 65 |       url: "#",
 66 |       type: "contract" as const,
 67 |       uploadedAt: new Date().toISOString()
 68 |     };
 69 |     
 70 |     setDocuments([...documents, mockDocument]);
 71 |   };
 72 |   
 73 |   return (
 74 |     <div className="space-y-8">
 75 |       <div>
 76 |         <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold">Business Commitment</h2>
 77 |         <p className="text-gray-500 mt-1">Create a business agreement with contract documents</p>
 78 |       </div>
 79 |       
 80 |       <Form {...form}>
 81 |         <form onSubmit={form.handleSubmit(handleSubmit)} className="space-y-6">
 82 |           <FormField
 83 |             control={form.control}
 84 |             name="title"
 85 |             render={({ field }) => (
 86 |               <FormItem>
 87 |                 <FormLabel>Agreement Title</FormLabel>
 88 |                 <FormControl>
 89 |                   <Input placeholder="Title of your business agreement" {...field} />
 90 |                 </FormControl>
 91 |                 <FormMessage />
 92 |               </FormItem>
 93 |             )}
 94 |           />
 95 |           
 96 |           <FormField
 97 |             control={form.control}
 98 |             name="description"
 99 |             render={({ field }) => (
100 |               <FormItem>
101 |                 <FormLabel>Description</FormLabel>
102 |                 <FormControl>
103 |                   <Textarea 
104 |                     placeholder="Describe the business agreement details..."
105 |                     className="min-h-[120px]" 
106 |                     {...field} 
107 |                   />
108 |                 </FormControl>
109 |                 <FormMessage />
110 |               </FormItem>
111 |             )}
112 |           />
113 |           
114 |           <FormField
115 |             control={form.control}
116 |             name="terms"
117 |             render={({ field }) => (
118 |               <FormItem>
119 |                 <FormLabel>Terms & Conditions</FormLabel>
120 |                 <FormControl>
121 |                   <Textarea 
122 |                     placeholder="Enter terms and conditions of the agreement..."
123 |                     className="min-h-[150px]" 
124 |                     {...field} 
125 |                   />
126 |                 </FormControl>
127 |                 <FormDescription>
128 |                   Detail the specific terms of this business agreement
129 |                 </FormDescription>
130 |                 <FormMessage />
131 |               </FormItem>
132 |             )}
133 |           />
134 |           
135 |           <FormField
136 |             control={form.control}
137 |             name="value"
138 |             render={({ field }) => (
139 |               <FormItem>
140 |                 <FormLabel>Agreement Value (Optional)</FormLabel>
141 |                 <FormControl>
142 |                   <Input 
143 |                     type="number"
144 |                     placeholder="Enter monetary value" 
145 |                     {...field} 
146 |                   />
147 |                 </FormControl>

150 |                 </FormDescription>
151 |                 <FormMessage />
152 |               </FormItem>
153 |             )}
154 |           />
155 |           
156 |           <FormField
157 |             control={form.control}
158 |             name="deadline"
159 |             render={({ field }) => (
160 |               <FormItem className="flex flex-col">
161 |                 <FormLabel>Deadline/Expiry Date</FormLabel>
162 |                 <Popover>

164 |                     <FormControl>
165 |                       <Button
166 |                         variant={"outline"}
167 |                         className={`w-full justify-start text-left font-normal ${!field.value && "text-muted-foreground"}`}
168 |                       >
169 |                         <CalendarIcon className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
170 |                         {field.value ? format(field.value, "PPP") : <span>Pick a date</span>}
171 |                       </Button>
172 |                     </FormControl>
173 |                   </PopoverTrigger>
174 |                   <PopoverContent className="w-auto p-0" align="start">
175 |                     <Calendar
176 |                       mode="single"
177 |                       selected={field.value}
178 |                       onSelect={field.onChange}
179 |                       initialFocus
180 |                     />
181 |                   </PopoverContent>
182 |                 </Popover>
183 |                 <FormDescription>
184 |                   Set a deadline or expiry date for this agreement
185 |                 </FormDescription>
186 |                 <FormMessage />
187 |               </FormItem>
188 |             )}
189 |           />
190 |           
191 |           {/* Document Upload Section */}
192 |           <div className="space-y-4 p-4 border rounded-lg">
193 |             <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
194 |               <h3 className="font-medium">Related Documents</h3>

196 |                 <Upload className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
197 |                 Upload Document
198 |               </Button>
199 |             </div>
200 |             
201 |             {documents.length > 0 ? (
202 |               <div className="space-y-2">

204 |                   <div key={index} className="flex items-center justify-between p-2 border rounded">
205 |                     <div>

210 |                     </div>

212 |                       <Button size="sm" variant="outline">View</Button>

214 |                     </div>
215 |                   </div>
216 |                 ))}
217 |               </div>
218 |             ) : (
219 |               <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm">No documents uploaded yet</p>

110 |                   flex items-center mt-2 text-sm font-medium 
111 |                   transition-opacity duration-300 
112 |                   ${hoveredType === item.type ? 'opacity-100' : 'opacity-70'}
113 |                 `}
114 |               >
115 |                 <span>Select</span>
116 |                 <ChevronRight className="ml-1 h-4 w-4" />
117 |               </div>
118 |             </div>
119 |           </motion.div>
120 |         ))}
121 |       </div>
122 |     </div>

 15 | interface ContractCommitmentFormProps {
 16 |   onSubmit: (data: Partial<ContractCommitment>) => void;
 17 | }
 18 | 
 19 | const ContractCommitmentForm = ({ onSubmit }: ContractCommitmentFormProps) => {
 20 |   const navigate = useNavigate();
 21 |   const { toast } = useToast();
 22 |   const [title, setTitle] = useState("");
 23 |   const [description, setDescription] = useState("");
 24 |   const [contractType, setContractType] = useState<string>("sponsorship");
 25 |   const [contractDetails, setContractDetails] = useState("");
 26 |   const [deadline, setDeadline] = useState("");
 27 |   const [taggedUsers, setTaggedUsers] = useState<{ id: string; name: string; role: "associated" | "informed" }[]>([]);
 28 |   const [documents, setDocuments] = useState<{ name: string; url: string; uploadedAt: string }[]>([]);
 29 | 
 30 |   const handleAddDocument = (doc: { name: string; url: string }) => {
 31 |     setDocuments([
 32 |       ...documents,
 33 |       {
 34 |         ...doc,
 35 |         uploadedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
 36 |       },
 37 |     ]);
 38 |     
 39 |     toast({
 40 |       title: "Document Added",
 41 |       description: `${doc.name} has been added to your commitment.`,
 42 |     });
 43 |   };
 44 | 
 45 |   const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
 46 |     e.preventDefault();
 47 | 
 48 |     if (!title) {
 49 |       toast({
 50 |         title: "Error",
 51 |         description: "Please enter a title for your commitment.",
 52 |         variant: "destructive",
 53 |       });
 54 |       return;
 55 |     }
 56 | 
 57 |     // Prepare data for submission
 58 |     const contractCommitment: Partial<ContractCommitment> = {
 59 |       type: "contract",
 60 |       title,
 61 |       description,
 62 |       contractType: contractType as "sponsorship" | "employment" | "service" | "termsheet" | "other",
 63 |       contractDetails,
 64 |       deadline,
 65 |       parties: [
 66 |         {
 67 |           id: "current-user", // This would be replaced with actual user ID
 68 |           name: "You",
 69 |           role: "associated"
 70 |         },
 71 |         ...taggedUsers,
 72 |       ],
 73 |       documents,
 74 |       status: "pending",
 75 |       createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
 76 |       createdBy: "current-user", // This would be replaced with actual user ID
 77 |     };
 78 | 
 79 |     onSubmit(contractCommitment);
 80 |   };
 81 |   
 82 |   return (
 83 |     <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-8">
 84 |       <div className="space-y-2">
 85 |         <Label htmlFor="title">Title</Label>
 86 |         <Input
 87 |           id="title"
 88 |           placeholder="Enter the contract title"
 89 |           value={title}
 90 |           onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
 91 |           className="glow-effect"
 92 |         />
 93 |       </div>
 94 |       
 95 |       <div className="space-y-2">
 96 |         <Label htmlFor="description">Description</Label>

 98 |           id="description"
 99 |           placeholder="Describe the contract commitment"
100 |           value={description}
101 |           onChange={(e) => setDescription(e.target.value)}

103 |         />

110 |             <SelectTrigger className="glow-effect">
111 |               <SelectValue placeholder="Select contract type" />
112 |             </SelectTrigger>

114 |               <SelectItem value="sponsorship">Sponsorship Agreement</SelectItem>

119 |             </SelectContent>
120 |           </Select>
121 |         </div>

124 |           <Label htmlFor="deadline">Deadline</Label>
125 |           <Input
126 |             id="deadline"
127 |             type="date"
128 |             value={deadline}
129 |             onChange={(e) => setDeadline(e.target.value)}
130 |             className="glow-effect"
131 |           />
132 |         </div>
133 |       </div>
134 |       
135 |       <div className="space-y-2">
136 |         <Label htmlFor="contractDetails">Contract Details</Label>
137 |         <Textarea
138 |           id="contractDetails"
139 |           placeholder="Enter specific terms, conditions, and details of the contract"
140 |           value={contractDetails}
141 |           onChange={(e) => setContractDetails(e.target.value)}
142 |           className="min-h-[150px] glow-effect"
143 |         />
144 |       </div>

154 |         />

162 |         <FileUpload onFileUpload={handleAddDocument} supportedTypes={".pdf,.doc,.docx,.txt"} />
163 |

168 |               {documents.map((doc, index) => (

171 |                     <p className="font-medium">{doc.name}</p>
172 |                     <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">
173 |                       Uploaded {new Date(doc.uploadedAt).toLocaleString()}
174 |                     </p>
175 |                   </div>
176 |                   <Button
177 |                     type="button"
178 |                     variant="ghost"
179 |                     size="sm"
180 |                     onClick={() => {
181 |                       setDocuments(documents.filter((_, i) => i !== index));
182 |                     }}
183 |                   >
184 |                     Remove
185 |                   </Button>
186 |                 </div>
187 |               ))}
188 |             </div>
189 |           </div>
190 |         )}
191 |       </div>

200 |         </Button>

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/src/components/commitment/FileUpload.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1 | 
  2 | import { useState } from "react";
  3 | import { FileUp, FileCheck, X, Loader2 } from "lucide-react";
  4 | import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
  5 | import { toast } from "sonner";
  6 | 
  7 | interface FileUploadProps {
  8 |   onFileUpload: (file: { name: string; url: string; type?: string }) => void;
  9 |   supportedTypes?: string;
 10 |   maxSize?: number; // in MB
 11 | }
 12 | 
 13 | const FileUpload = ({ 
 14 |   onFileUpload, 
 15 |   supportedTypes = ".pdf,.doc,.docx,.txt,.png,.jpg,.jpeg", 
 16 |   maxSize = 5 
 17 | }: FileUploadProps) => {
 18 |   const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
 19 |   const [isUploading, setIsUploading] = useState(false);
 20 |   
 21 |   // In a real app, this would upload to a storage service
 22 |   const mockUpload = (file: File): Promise<string> => {
 23 |     return new Promise((resolve) => {
 24 |       // Simulate upload delay
 25 |       setTimeout(() => {
 26 |         // Create a mock URL (in production this would be a real URL)
 27 |         const mockUrl = `https://example.com/uploads/${encodeURIComponent(file.name)}`;
 28 |         resolve(mockUrl);
 29 |       }, 1000);
 30 |     });
 31 |   };
 32 |   
 33 |   const handleDragOver = (e: React.DragEvent) => {
 34 |     e.preventDefault();
 35 |     setIsDragging(true);
 36 |   };
 37 |   
 38 |   const handleDragLeave = (e: React.DragEvent) => {
 39 |     e.preventDefault();
 40 |     setIsDragging(false);
 41 |   };
 42 |   
 43 |   const handleDrop = (e: React.DragEvent) => {
 44 |     e.preventDefault();
 45 |     setIsDragging(false);
 46 |     
 47 |     const files = e.dataTransfer.files;
 48 |     if (files.length > 0) {
 49 |       handleFileSelection(files[0]);
 50 |     }
 51 |   };
 52 |   
 53 |   const handleFileChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
 54 |     if (e.target.files && e.target.files.length > 0) {
 55 |       handleFileSelection(e.target.files[0]);
 56 |     }
 57 |   };
 58 |   
 59 |   const handleFileSelection = async (file: File) => {
 60 |     // Validate file type
 61 |     const fileExtension = `.${file.name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase()}`;
 62 |     const isValidType = supportedTypes.includes(fileExtension);
 63 |     
 64 |     if (!isValidType) {
 65 |       toast.error(`Invalid file type. Supported types: ${supportedTypes}`);
 66 |       return;
 67 |     }
 68 |     
 69 |     // Validate file size
 70 |     const fileSizeInMB = file.size / (1024 * 1024);
 71 |     if (fileSizeInMB > maxSize) {
 72 |       toast.error(`File too large. Maximum size: ${maxSize}MB`);
 73 |       return;
 74 |     }
 75 |     
 76 |     // Upload file
 77 |     setIsUploading(true);
 78 |     try {
 79 |       const fileUrl = await mockUpload(file);
 80 |       
 81 |       onFileUpload({
 82 |         name: file.name,
 83 |         url: fileUrl,
 84 |         type: file.type,
 85 |       });
 86 |       
 87 |       toast.success("File uploaded successfully!");
 88 |     } catch (error) {
 89 |       console.error("Upload error:", error);
 90 |       toast.error("Failed to upload file. Please try again.");
 91 |     } finally {
 92 |       setIsUploading(false);
 93 |     }
 94 |   };
 95 |   
 96 |   return (
 97 |     <div
 98 |       className={`border-2 border-dashed rounded-lg p-8 text-center transition-colors ${
 99 |         isDragging 
100 |           ? "border-connect-400 bg-connect-50 dark:bg-connect-900/10" 
101 |           : "border-gray-300 dark:border-gray-700"
102 |       } glow-effect`}
103 |       onDragOver={handleDragOver}
104 |       onDragLeave={handleDragLeave}
105 |       onDrop={handleDrop}
106 |     >
107 |       {isUploading ? (
108 |         <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-4">
109 |           <Loader2 className="h-10 w-10 text-connect-500 animate-spin mb-4" />
110 |           <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300">Uploading file...</p>
111 |         </div>
112 |       ) : (
113 |         <>
114 |           <FileUp className="h-10 w-10 text-gray-400 mx-auto mb-4" />
115 |           <p className="mb-2 text-sm text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300">
116 |             <span className="font-semibold">Click to upload</span> or drag and drop
117 |           </p>
118 |           <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">
119 |             {supportedTypes} (Max {maxSize}MB)
120 |           </p>
121 |           <input
122 |             type="file"
123 |             className="hidden"
124 |             accept={supportedTypes}
125 |             onChange={handleFileChange}
126 |             id="file-upload"
127 |           />
128 |           <label htmlFor="file-upload" className="mt-4 inline-block">
129 |             <Button 
130 |               type="button" 
131 |               variant="outline"
132 |               className="text-connect-500 border-connect-500"
133 |             >
134 |               <FileCheck className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
135 |               Select File
136 |             </Button>
137 |           </label>
138 |         </>
139 |       )}
140 |     </div>
141 |   );
142 | };
143 | 
144 | export default FileUpload;
145 |

/src/components/commitment/PersonalCommitmentForm.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1 | 
  2 | import { useState } from "react";
  3 | import { useForm } from "react-hook-form";
  4 | import { zodResolver } from "@hookform/resolvers/zod";
  5 | import * as z from "zod";
  6 | import { PersonalCommitment, TaggedUser } from "@/types/commitments";
  7 | import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
  8 | import { Calendar } from "@/components/ui/calendar";
  9 | import { Popover, PopoverContent, PopoverTrigger } from "@/components/ui/popover";
 10 | import { CalendarIcon } from "lucide-react";
 11 | import { format } from "date-fns";
 12 | import { Switch } from "@/components/ui/switch";
 13 | import { 
 14 |   Form, 
 15 |   FormControl, 
 16 |   FormDescription, 
 17 |   FormField, 
 18 |   FormItem, 
 19 |   FormLabel, 
 20 |   FormMessage 
 21 | } from "@/components/ui/form";
 22 | import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
 23 | import { Textarea } from "@/components/ui/textarea";
 24 | import UserTagsInput from "./UserTagsInput";
 25 | 
 26 | const formSchema = z.object({
 27 |   title: z.string().min(3, "Title must be at least 3 characters"),
 28 |   description: z.string().min(10, "Description must be at least 10 characters"),
 29 |   goal: z.string().min(5, "Goal must be at least 5 characters"),
 30 |   milestone: z.string().optional(),
 31 |   deadline: z.date().optional(),
 32 |   isPublic: z.boolean().default(false)
 33 | });
 34 | 
 35 | interface PersonalCommitmentFormProps {
 36 |   onSubmit: (data: Partial<PersonalCommitment>) => void;
 37 | }
 38 | 
 39 | const PersonalCommitmentForm = ({ onSubmit }: PersonalCommitmentFormProps) => {
 40 |   const [taggedUsers, setTaggedUsers] = useState<TaggedUser[]>([]);
 41 |   
 42 |   const form = useForm<z.infer<typeof formSchema>>({
 43 |     resolver: zodResolver(formSchema),
 44 |     defaultValues: {
 45 |       title: "",
 46 |       description: "",
 47 |       goal: "",
 48 |       milestone: "",
 49 |       isPublic: false
 50 |     }
 51 |   });
 52 |   
 53 |   const handleSubmit = (values: z.infer<typeof formSchema>) => {
 54 |     const commitmentData: Partial<PersonalCommitment> = {
 55 |       ...values,
 56 |       type: "personal",
 57 |       parties: taggedUsers,
 58 |       status: "active",
 59 |       deadline: values.deadline ? format(values.deadline, "yyyy-MM-dd") : undefined
 60 |     };
 61 |     
 62 |     onSubmit(commitmentData);
 63 |   };
 64 |   
 65 |   return (
 66 |     <div className="space-y-8">
 67 |       <div>
 68 |         <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold">Personal Commitment</h2>
 69 |         <p className="text-gray-500 mt-1">Create a commitment for your personal goals and ambitions</p>
 70 |       </div>
 71 |       
 72 |       <Form {...form}>
 73 |         <form onSubmit={form.handleSubmit(handleSubmit)} className="space-y-6">
 74 |           <FormField
 75 |             control={form.control}
 76 |             name="title"
 77 |             render={({ field }) => (
 78 |               <FormItem>
 79 |                 <FormLabel>Title</FormLabel>
 80 |                 <FormControl>
 81 |                   <Input placeholder="Title of your commitment" {...field} />
 82 |                 </FormControl>
 83 |                 <FormMessage />
 84 |               </FormItem>
 85 |             )}
 86 |           />
 87 |           
 88 |           <FormField
 89 |             control={form.control}
 90 |             name="description"
 91 |             render={({ field }) => (
 92 |               <FormItem>
 93 |                 <FormLabel>Description</FormLabel>
 94 |                 <FormControl>
 95 |                   <Textarea 
 96 |                     placeholder="Describe your commitment in detail..."
 97 |                     className="min-h-[120px]" 
 98 |                     {...field} 
 99 |                   />
100 |                 </FormControl>
101 |                 <FormMessage />
102 |               </FormItem>
103 |             )}
104 |           />
105 |           
106 |           <FormField
107 |             control={form.control}
108 |             name="goal"
109 |             render={({ field }) => (
110 |               <FormItem>
111 |                 <FormLabel>Goal</FormLabel>
112 |                 <FormControl>
113 |                   <Input placeholder="What's your specific goal?" {...field} />
114 |                 </FormControl>
115 |                 <FormDescription>
116 |                   Clearly define what you want to achieve with this commitment
117 |                 </FormDescription>
118 |                 <FormMessage />
119 |               </FormItem>
120 |             )}
121 |           />
122 |           
123 |           <FormField
124 |             control={form.control}
125 |             name="milestone"
126 |             render={({ field }) => (
127 |               <FormItem>
128 |                 <FormLabel>Milestone (Optional)</FormLabel>
129 |                 <FormControl>

131 |                 </FormControl>

134 |                 </FormDescription>

136 |               </FormItem>
137 |             )}
138 |           />
139 |           
140 |           <FormField
141 |             control={form.control}
142 |             name="deadline"
143 |             render={({ field }) => (
144 |               <FormItem className="flex flex-col">
145 |                 <FormLabel>Deadline</FormLabel>
146 |                 <Popover>
147 |                   <PopoverTrigger asChild>

150 |                         variant={"outline"}

152 |                       >
153 |                         <CalendarIcon className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />

155 |                       </Button>
156 |                     </FormControl>
157 |                   </PopoverTrigger>
158 |                   <PopoverContent className="w-auto p-0" align="start">

164 |                     />
165 |                   </PopoverContent>

181 |                   <FormLabel className="text-base">Public Commitment</FormLabel>
182 |                   <FormDescription>
183 |                     Make this commitment visible to everyone
184 |                   </FormDescription>
185 |                 </div>

188 |                     checked={field.value}

190 |                   />
191 |                 </FormControl>
192 |               </FormItem>
193 |             )}
194 |           />

/src/components/commitment/TrustCommitmentForm.tsx:

  1 | 
  2 | import { useState } from "react";
  3 | import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
  4 | import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
  5 | import { TrustCommitment } from "@/types/commitments";
  6 | import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
  7 | import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
  8 | import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
  9 | import { Textarea } from "@/components/ui/textarea";
 10 | import { RadioGroup, RadioGroupItem } from "@/components/ui/radio-group";
 11 | import UserTagsInput from "./UserTagsInput";
 12 | import { Lock, FileKey, Users, FlaskRound } from "lucide-react";
 13 | 
 14 | interface TrustCommitmentFormProps {
 15 |   onSubmit: (data: Partial<TrustCommitment>) => void;
 16 | }
 17 | 
 18 | const TrustCommitmentForm = ({ onSubmit }: TrustCommitmentFormProps) => {
 19 |   const navigate = useNavigate();
 20 |   const { toast } = useToast();
 21 |   const [title, setTitle] = useState("");
 22 |   const [description, setDescription] = useState("");
 23 |   const [secretText, setSecretText] = useState("");
 24 |   const [trustLevel, setTrustLevel] = useState<"low" | "medium" | "high">("medium");
 25 |   const [taggedUsers, setTaggedUsers] = useState<{ id: string; name: string; role: "associated" | "informed" }[]>([]);
 26 | 
 27 |   // Mock encryption function (in a real app, this would use actual encryption)
 28 |   const encryptSecret = (text: string) => {
 29 |     return btoa(text); // Base64 encoding for demonstration
 30 |   };
 31 | 
 32 |   const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
 33 |     e.preventDefault();
 34 | 
 35 |     if (!title || !secretText) {
 36 |       toast({
 37 |         title: "Error",
 38 |         description: "Please fill in all required fields.",
 39 |         variant: "destructive",
 40 |       });
 41 |       return;
 42 |     }
 43 | 
 44 |     if (taggedUsers.length === 0) {
 45 |       toast({
 46 |         title: "Error",
 47 |         description: "Please tag at least one person to share this trust with.",
 48 |         variant: "destructive",
 49 |       });
 50 |       return;
 51 |     }
 52 | 
 53 |     // Encrypt the secret
 54 |     const encryptedSecret = encryptSecret(secretText);
 55 | 
 56 |     // Prepare data for submission
 57 |     const trustCommitment: Partial<TrustCommitment> = {
 58 |       type: "trust",
 59 |       title,
 60 |       description,
 61 |       secretEncrypted: encryptedSecret,
 62 |       trustLevel,
 63 |       parties: [
 64 |         {
 65 |           id: "current-user", // This would be replaced with actual user ID
 66 |           name: "You",
 67 |           role: "associated"
 68 |         },
 69 |         ...taggedUsers,
 70 |       ],
 71 |       status: "active", // Trust commitments are active immediately
 72 |       createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
 73 |       createdBy: "current-user", // This would be replaced with actual user ID
 74 |     };
 75 | 
 76 |     onSubmit(trustCommitment);
 77 |   };
 78 |   
 79 |   return (
 80 |     <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-8">
 81 |       <div className="text-center mb-6">
 82 |         <Lock className="h-12 w-12 mx-auto mb-2 text-connect-500" />
 83 |         <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold">Trust Commitment</h2>
 84 |         <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Share a secret with trusted individuals</p>
 85 |       </div>
 86 |       
 87 |       <div className="space-y-2">
 88 |         <Label htmlFor="title">Title</Label>
 89 |         <Input
 90 |           id="title"
 91 |           placeholder="Give this trust commitment a title"
 92 |           value={title}
 93 |           onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
 94 |           className="glow-effect"
 95 |         />
 96 |       </div>
 97 |       
 98 |       <div className="space-y-2">
 99 |         <Label htmlFor="description">Description</Label>
100 |         <Textarea
101 |           id="description"
102 |           placeholder="Describe the nature of this trust (visible to all parties)"
103 |           value={description}
104 |           onChange={(e) => setDescription(e.target.value)}
105 |           className="min-h-[100px] glow-effect"
106 |         />
107 |       </div>
108 |       
109 |       <div className="space-y-2">
110 |         <Label htmlFor="secretText" className="flex items-center">
111 |           <FileKey className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
112 |           The Secret
113 |         </Label>
114 |         <div className="relative">
115 |           <Textarea
116 |             id="secretText"
117 |             placeholder="Enter the secret information to be encrypted"
118 |             value={secretText}
119 |             onChange={(e) => setSecretText(e.target.value)}
120 |             className="min-h-[100px] pr-10 glow-effect"
121 |           />
122 |           <div className="absolute right-3 top-3 text-connect-500">
123 |             <Lock className="h-5 w-5" />
124 |           </div>
125 |         </div>
126 |         <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">
127 |           This information will be encrypted and only visible to tagged users when unlocked
128 |         </p>
129 |       </div>
130 |       
131 |       <div className="space-y-2">
132 |         <Label className="flex items-center">
133 |           <Users className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
134 |           Share Secret With
135 |         </Label>
136 |         <UserTagsInput 
137 |           onTagsChange={setTaggedUsers} 
138 |           className="glow-effect"
139 |         />
140 |       </div>
141 |       
142 |       <div className="space-y-2">
143 |         <Label className="flex items-center">
144 |           <FlaskRound className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
145 |           Trust Level
146 |         </Label>
147 |         <RadioGroup value={trustLevel} onValueChange={(val) => setTrustLevel(val as "low" | "medium" | "high")} className="flex space-x-4">
148 |           <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
149 |             <RadioGroupItem value="low" id="low" />
150 |             <Label htmlFor="low">Low</Label>
151 |           </div>

157 |             <RadioGroupItem value="high" id="high" />
158 |             <Label htmlFor="high">High</Label>
159 |           </div>
160 |         </RadioGroup>
161 |       </div>
162 |       
163 |       <div className="p-4 bg-yellow-50 dark:bg-yellow-900/30 rounded-lg border border-yellow-100 dark:border-yellow-800">
164 |         <p className="text-sm text-yellow-800 dark:text-yellow-200">
165 |           <strong>Important:</strong> Trust commitments use 2x2 multisig encryption. 
166 |           The secret can only be decrypted when both you and the recipient agree to unlock it.
167 |           This creates an immutable record of trust between parties.
168 |         </p>
169 |       </div>
170 |       
171 |       <div className="flex justify-end space-x-4">
172 |         <Button 
173 |           type="button" 
174 |           variant="outline"
175 |           onClick={() => navigate("/dashboard")}
176 |         >
177 |           Cancel
178 |         </Button>
179 |         <Button type="submit" className="bg-connect-500 hover:bg-connect-600">
