  1 | import { useParams, useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
  2 | import { useState, useEffect } from "react";
  3 | import Navbar from "@/components/Navbar";
  4 | import Footer from "@/components/Footer";
  5 | import { 
  6 |   Card, 
  7 |   CardContent, 
  8 |   CardDescription, 
  9 |   CardFooter, 
 10 |   CardHeader, 
 11 |   CardTitle 
 12 | } from "@/components/ui/card";
 13 | import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
 14 | import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
 15 | import { 
 16 |   ArrowLeft, 
 17 |   Calendar, 
 18 |   Users, 
 19 |   Clock, 
 20 |   CheckCircle, 
 21 |   AlertCircle,
 22 |   FileText,
 23 |   User,
 24 |   Briefcase,
 25 |   BookOpen,
 26 |   Handshake,
 27 |   Heart,
 28 |   Lock
 29 | } from "lucide-react";
 30 | import { CommitmentType, Commitment, TrustCommitment } from "@/types/commitments";
 31 | 
 32 | const CommitmentDetails = () => {
 33 |   const { id } = useParams<{ id: string }>();
 34 |   const navigate = useNavigate();
 35 |   const [commitment, setCommitment] = useState<Partial<Commitment> | null>(null);
 36 |   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
 37 |   
 38 |   useEffect(() => {
 39 |     if (id) {
 40 |       console.log("Looking for commitment with ID:", id);
 41 |       // Try to get the commitment data from sessionStorage using the exact ID
 42 |       const storedCommitment = sessionStorage.getItem(id);
 43 |       
 44 |       if (storedCommitment) {
 45 |         try {
 46 |           const parsedCommitment = JSON.parse(storedCommitment);
 47 |           console.log("Found commitment:", parsedCommitment);
 48 |           setCommitment(parsedCommitment);
 49 |         } catch (error) {
 50 |           console.error("Error parsing commitment data:", error);
 51 |         }
 52 |       } else {
 53 |         console.error("No commitment found with ID:", id);
 54 |       }
 55 |       setLoading(false);
 56 |     }
 57 |   }, [id]);
 58 |   
 59 |   if (loading) {
 60 |     return (
 61 |       <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center">
 62 |         <p>Loading commitment details...</p>
 63 |       </div>
 64 |     );
 65 |   }
 66 |   
 67 |   if (!commitment) {
 68 |     return (
 69 |       <div className="min-h-screen flex flex-col bg-gradient-to-b from-gray-50 to-gray-100 dark:from-gray-900 dark:to-gray-800">
 70 |         <Navbar />
 71 |         <main className="flex-grow flex items-center justify-center">
 72 |           <Card className="w-full max-w-md">
 73 |             <CardHeader>
 74 |               <CardTitle>Commitment Not Found</CardTitle>
 75 |               <CardDescription>The commitment you're looking for doesn't exist or has been removed.</CardDescription>
 76 |             </CardHeader>
 77 |             <CardFooter>
 78 |               <Button onClick={() => navigate("/dashboard")}>Back to Dashboard</Button>
 79 |             </CardFooter>
 80 |           </Card>
 81 |         </main>
 82 |         <Footer />
 83 |       </div>
 84 |     );
 85 |   }
 86 |   
 87 |   const getStatusColor = (status: string = "active") => {
 88 |     switch (status) {
 89 |       case "active":
 90 |         return "bg-green-100 text-green-800 dark:bg-green-900/30 dark:text-green-300";
 91 |       case "pending":
 92 |         return "bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800 dark:bg-yellow-900/30 dark:text-yellow-300";
 93 |       case "completed":
 94 |         return "bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 dark:bg-blue-900/30 dark:text-blue-300";
 95 |       case "expired":
 96 |         return "bg-red-100 text-red-800 dark:bg-red-900/30 dark:text-red-300";
 97 |       default:
 98 |         return "bg-gray-100 text-gray-800 dark:bg-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300";
 99 |     }
100 |   };
101 | 
102 |   const getTypeIcon = (type: CommitmentType = "personal") => {
103 |     switch (type) {
104 |       case "personal":
105 |         return <User className="h-5 w-5" />;
106 |       case "business":
107 |         return <Briefcase className="h-5 w-5" />;
108 |       case "contract":
109 |         return <FileText className="h-5 w-5" />;
110 |       case "religious":
111 |         return <BookOpen className="h-5 w-5" />;
112 |       case "promise":
113 |         return <Handshake className="h-5 w-5" />;
114 |       case "friendly":
115 |         return <Heart className="h-5 w-5" />;
116 |       case "trust":
117 |         return <Lock className="h-5 w-5" />;
118 |       default:
119 |         return <CheckCircle className="h-5 w-5" />;
120 |     }
121 |   };
122 | 
123 |   const decryptSecret = () => {
124 |     const encryptedText = (commitment as TrustCommitment).secretEncrypted;
125 |     return atob(encryptedText || ""); // Simple base64 decode for demo
126 |   };
127 | 
128 |   const getTypeColor = (type: CommitmentType = "personal") => {
129 |     switch (type) {
130 |       case "personal":
131 |         return "bg-blue-100 text-blue-600 dark:bg-blue-900/30 dark:text-blue-400";
132 |       case "business":
133 |         return "bg-purple-100 text-purple-600 dark:bg-purple-900/30 dark:text-purple-400";
134 |       case "contract":
135 |         return "bg-gray-100 text-gray-600 dark:bg-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300";
136 |       case "religious":
137 |         return "bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-600 dark:bg-yellow-900/30 dark:text-yellow-400";
138 |       case "promise":
139 |         return "bg-green-100 text-green-600 dark:bg-green-900/30 dark:text-green-400";
140 |       case "friendly":
141 |         return "bg-pink-100 text-pink-600 dark:bg-pink-900/30 dark:text-pink-400";
142 |       case "trust":
143 |         return "bg-red-100 text-red-600 dark:bg-red-900/30 dark:text-red-400";
144 |       default:
145 |         return "bg-blue-100 text-blue-600 dark:bg-blue-900/30 dark:text-blue-400";
146 |     }
147 |   };
148 |   
149 |   return (
150 |     <div className="min-h-screen flex flex-col bg-gradient-to-b from-gray-50 to-gray-100 dark:from-gray-900 dark:to-gray-800">
151 |       <Navbar />
152 |       
153 |       <main className="flex-grow py-8">
154 |         <div className="connect-container">
155 |           <Button 
156 |             variant="ghost" 
157 |             className="mb-6 group hover:bg-white/80 dark:hover:bg-gray-800/80" 
158 |             onClick={() => navigate("/dashboard")}
159 |           >
160 |             <ArrowLeft className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 transition-transform group-hover:-translate-x-1" />
161 |             Back to Dashboard
162 |           </Button>
163 |           
164 |           <Card className="shadow-lg border-0 overflow-hidden artful-card">
165 |             <CardHeader className="pb-4 bg-gradient-to-r from-gray-50 to-white dark:from-gray-800 dark:to-gray-900">
166 |               <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
167 |                 <div className="flex items-start gap-4">
168 |                   <div className={`p-3 rounded-full ${getTypeColor(commitment.type as CommitmentType)}`}>
169 |                     {getTypeIcon(commitment.type as CommitmentType)}
170 |                   </div>
171 |                   <div className="space-y-1">
172 |                     <CardTitle className="text-2xl">{commitment.title}</CardTitle>
173 |                     <CardDescription>
174 |                       {commitment.type ? (commitment.type.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + commitment.type.slice(1)) : "Personal"} Commitment
175 |                     </CardDescription>
176 |                   </div>
177 |                 </div>
178 |                 <Badge className={getStatusColor(commitment.status)}>
179 |                   {commitment.status ? (commitment.status.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + commitment.status.slice(1)) : "Active"}
180 |                 </Badge>
181 |               </div>
182 |             </CardHeader>
183 |             
184 |             <CardContent className="space-y-6 p-6">
185 |               <div>
186 |                 <h3 className="text-lg font-medium mb-2">Description</h3>
187 |                 <p className="text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300">{commitment.description}</p>
188 |               </div>
189 |               
190 |               <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
191 |                 <div className="flex items-center gap-3 p-4 bg-gray-50 dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-lg transition-all hover:shadow-md">
192 |                   <Calendar className="h-5 w-5 text-connect-500" />
193 |                   <div>
194 |                     <p className="text-sm font-medium">Created On</p>
195 |                     <p>{commitment.createdAt ? new Date(commitment.createdAt).toLocaleDateString() : "N/A"}</p>
196 |                   </div>
197 |                 </div>
198 |                 
199 |                 <div className="flex items-center gap-3 p-4 bg-gray-50 dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-lg transition-all hover:shadow-md">
200 |                   <Clock className="h-5 w-5 text-connect-500" />
201 |                   <div>
202 |                     <p className="text-sm font-medium">Deadline</p>
203 |                     <p>{commitment.deadline ? new Date(commitment.deadline).toLocaleDateString() : "No deadline"}</p>
204 |                   </div>
205 |                 </div>
206 |               </div>
207 |               
208 |               {commitment.parties && commitment.parties.length > 0 && (
209 |                 <div>
210 |                   <h3 className="text-lg font-medium mb-2">Involved Parties</h3>
211 |                   <div className="space-y-2">
212 |                     {commitment.parties.map((party, index) => (
213 |                       <div 
214 |                         key={index} 
215 |                         className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border rounded-lg glow-effect"
216 |                       >
217 |                         <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
218 |                           <div className={`
219 |                             h-10 w-10 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-white
220 |                             ${party.role === "associated" ? "bg-connect-500" : "bg-gray-400 dark:bg-gray-600"}
221 |                           `}>
222 |                             {party.name ? party.name.charAt(0) : "?"}
223 |                           </div>
224 |                           <span>{party.name}</span>
225 |                         </div>
226 |                         <Badge variant={party.role === "associated" ? "default" : "outline"} className="capitalize">
227 |                           {party.role}
228 |                         </Badge>
229 |                       </div>
230 |                     ))}
231 |                   </div>
232 |                 </div>
233 |               )}
234 |               
235 |               {commitment.type === "trust" && (commitment as TrustCommitment).secretEncrypted && (
236 |                 <div className="p-6 border border-dotted rounded-lg bg-gradient-to-br from-gray-50 to-gray-100 dark:from-gray-800 dark:to-gray-900">
237 |                   <div className="text-center mb-4">
238 |                     <div className="inline-flex items-center justify-center p-3 bg-red-100 dark:bg-red-900/30 text-red-600 dark:text-red-400 rounded-full mb-2">
239 |                       <Lock className="h-6 w-6" />
240 |                     </div>
241 |                     <h3 className="text-lg font-medium">Encrypted Secret</h3>
242 |                     <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">
243 |                       This secret is encrypted and requires dual authorization to view
244 |                     </p>
245 |                   </div>
246 |                   
247 |                   <div className="flex justify-center mt-4">
248 |                     <Button 
249 |                       variant="outline" 
250 |                       className="border-red-200 hover:bg-red-50 dark:border-red-800 dark:hover:bg-red-900/20"
251 |                       onClick={() => {
252 |                         const secret = decryptSecret();
253 |                         alert(`The secret is: ${secret}`);
254 |                       }}
255 |                     >
256 |                       <FileText className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
257 |                       Request to Unlock Secret
258 |                     </Button>
259 |                   </div>
260 |                 </div>
261 |               )}
262 |               
263 |               {commitment.type === "religious" && (commitment as any).religion && (
264 |                 <div className="space-y-4">
265 |                   <div className="flex items-center gap-3 p-4 bg-yellow-50 dark:bg-yellow-900/20 rounded-lg">
266 |                     <BookOpen className="h-5 w-5 text-yellow-600 dark:text-yellow-400" />
267 |                     <div>
268 |                       <p className="text-sm font-medium">Religion</p>
269 |                       <p>{(commitment as any).religion}</p>
270 |                     </div>
271 |                   </div>
272 |                   
273 |                   {(commitment as any).deity && (
274 |                     <div className="flex items-center gap-3 p-4 bg-yellow-50 dark:bg-yellow-900/20 rounded-lg">
275 |                       <BookOpen className="h-5 w-5 text-yellow-600 dark:text-yellow-400" />
276 |                       <div>
277 |                         <p className="text-sm font-medium">Deity</p>
278 |                         <p>{(commitment as any).deity}</p>
279 |                       </div>
280 |                     </div>
281 |                   )}
282 |                 </div>
283 |               )}
284 | 
285 |               {commitment.type === "personal" && (commitment as any).goal && (
286 |                 <div className="p-4 bg-blue-50 dark:bg-blue-900/20 rounded-lg">
287 |                   <h3 className="font-medium mb-2">Goal</h3>
288 |                   <p>{(commitment as any).goal}</p>
289 |                 </div>
290 |               )}
291 | 
292 |               {commitment.type === "promise" && (commitment as any).promiseType && (
293 |                 <div className="p-4 bg-green-50 dark:bg-green-900/20 rounded-lg">
294 |                   <h3 className="font-medium mb-2">Promise Type</h3>
295 |                   <p className="capitalize">{(commitment as any).promiseType}</p>
296 |                 </div>
297 |               )}
298 |             </CardContent>
299 |             
300 |             <CardFooter className="flex justify-between p-6 bg-gradient-to-r from-gray-50 to-white dark:from-gray-800 dark:to-gray-900">
301 |               <Button variant="outline" className="border-gray-300 hover:bg-white dark:border-gray-700 dark:hover:bg-gray-800">
302 |                 Edit Commitment
303 |               </Button>
304 |               
305 |               {commitment.status === "active" && (
306 |                 <Button className="bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-700">
307 |                   <CheckCircle className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
308 |                   Mark as Completed
309 |                 </Button>
310 |               )}
311 |               
312 |               {commitment.status === "pending" && (
313 |                 <Button className="bg-connect-500 hover:bg-connect-600">
314 |                   <CheckCircle className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
315 |                   Approve Commitment
316 |                 </Button>
317 |               )}
318 |             </CardFooter>
319 |           </Card>
320 |         </div>
321 |       </main>
322 |       
323 |       <Footer />
324 |     </div>
325 |   );
326 | };
327 | 
328 | export default CommitmentDetails;

/src/pages/CreateCommitment.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1 | 
  2 | import { useState } from "react";
  3 | import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
  4 | import { toast } from "sonner";
  5 | import { CommitmentType, Commitment } from "@/types/commitments";
  6 | import Navbar from "@/components/Navbar";
  7 | import Footer from "@/components/Footer";
  8 | import CommitmentTypeSelector from "@/components/commitment/CommitmentTypeSelector";
  9 | import PersonalCommitmentForm from "@/components/commitment/PersonalCommitmentForm";
 10 | import BusinessCommitmentForm from "@/components/commitment/BusinessCommitmentForm";
 11 | import ContractCommitmentForm from "@/components/commitment/ContractCommitmentForm";
 12 | import ReligiousCommitmentForm from "@/components/commitment/ReligiousCommitmentForm";
 13 | import PromiseCommitmentForm from "@/components/commitment/PromiseCommitmentForm";
 14 | import FriendlyCommitmentForm from "@/components/commitment/FriendlyCommitmentForm";
 15 | import TrustCommitmentForm from "@/components/commitment/TrustCommitmentForm";
 16 | import { Card, CardContent } from "@/components/ui/card";
 17 | import { ArrowLeft } from "lucide-react";
 18 | 
 19 | const CreateCommitment = () => {
 20 |   const [selectedType, setSelectedType] = useState<CommitmentType | null>(null);
 21 |   const navigate = useNavigate();
 22 |   
 23 |   const handleTypeSelect = (type: CommitmentType) => {
 24 |     setSelectedType(type);
 25 |   };
 26 |   
 27 |   const handleSubmit = (data: Partial<Commitment>) => {
 28 |     console.log("Creating commitment:", data);
 29 |     
 30 |     // Generate a unique ID for the commitment
 31 |     const mockId = `commitment-${Date.now()}`;
 32 |     
 33 |     // Store the created commitment in sessionStorage for retrieval
 34 |     const commitmentData = {
 35 |       id: mockId,
 36 |       ...data,
 37 |       createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
 38 |     };
 39 |     
 40 |     // Store the commitment data with the full ID as the key
 41 |     sessionStorage.setItem(mockId, JSON.stringify(commitmentData));
 42 |     
 43 |     toast.success("Commitment Created", {
 44 |       description: `Your ${selectedType} commitment has been created successfully.`,
 45 |       action: {
 46 |         label: "View",
 47 |         onClick: () => {
 48 |           navigate(`/commitment/${mockId}`);
 49 |         },
 50 |       },
 51 |     });
 52 |     
 53 |     // Navigate to the new commitment details page
 54 |     setTimeout(() => {
 55 |       navigate(`/commitment/${mockId}`);
 56 |     }, 500);
 57 |   };
 58 |   
 59 |   const renderForm = () => {
 60 |     switch (selectedType) {
 61 |       case "personal":
 62 |         return <PersonalCommitmentForm onSubmit={handleSubmit} />;
 63 |       case "business":
 64 |         return <BusinessCommitmentForm onSubmit={handleSubmit} />;
 65 |       case "contract":
 66 |         return <ContractCommitmentForm onSubmit={handleSubmit} />;
 67 |       case "religious":
 68 |         return <ReligiousCommitmentForm onSubmit={handleSubmit} />;
 69 |       case "promise":
 70 |         return <PromiseCommitmentForm onSubmit={handleSubmit} />;
 71 |       case "friendly":
 72 |         return <FriendlyCommitmentForm onSubmit={handleSubmit} />;
 73 |       case "trust":
 74 |         return <TrustCommitmentForm onSubmit={handleSubmit} />;
 75 |       default:
 76 |         return null;
 77 |     }
 78 |   };
 79 |   
 80 |   return (
 81 |     <div className="min-h-screen flex flex-col bg-gradient-to-b from-earth-50 to-earth-100 dark:from-blue-900/30 dark:to-gray-800">
 82 |       <Navbar />
 83 |       
 84 |       <main className="flex-grow py-12">
 85 |         <div className="connect-container">
 86 |           <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-8 text-center bg-gradient-to-r from-nordic-600 to-nordic-500 bg-clip-text text-transparent">
 87 |             Create New Commitment
 88 |           </h1>
 89 |           
 90 |           <Card className="shadow-nordic border-0 overflow-hidden artful-card">
 91 |             <CardContent className="p-6 sm:p-8">
 92 |               {!selectedType ? (
 93 |                 <CommitmentTypeSelector onSelect={handleTypeSelect} />
 94 |               ) : (
 95 |                 <div className="animate-fade-in">
 96 |                   <button 
 97 |                     onClick={() => setSelectedType(null)}
 98 |                     className="text-nordic-500 mb-6 inline-flex items-center hover:underline"
 99 |                   >
100 |                     <ArrowLeft className="mr-1 h-4 w-4" />
101 |                     Back to commitment types
102 |                   </button>
103 |                   
104 |                   {renderForm()}
105 |                 </div>
106 |               )}
107 |             </CardContent>
108 |           </Card>
109 |         </div>
110 |       </main>
111 |       
112 |       <Footer />
113 |     </div>
114 |   );
115 | };
116 | 
117 | export default CreateCommitment;
118 |

198 |                 variant={selectedFilter === "business" ? "default" : "outline"} 
199 |                 size="sm"

203 |                 <Briefcase className="h-4 w-4 mr-1" />
204 |                 Business
205 |               </Button>
206 |               
207 |               <Button
208 |                 variant={selectedFilter === "contract" ? "default" : "outline"} 
209 |                 size="sm"

211 |                 className="glow-effect"
212 |               >
213 |                 <FileText className="h-4 w-4 mr-1" />
214 |                 Contract
215 |               </Button>
216 |               
217 |               <Button
218 |                 variant={selectedFilter === "religious" ? "default" : "outline"} 
219 |                 size="sm"

221 |                 className={`glow-effect ${selectedFilter === "religious" ? "bg-yellow-500 hover:bg-yellow-600" : ""}`}

255 |               </Button>

264 |               <TabsTrigger value="completed" className="glow-effect">Completed</TabsTrigger>
265 |             </TabsList>
266 |             
267 |             <TabsContent value="all" className="mt-0">
268 |               {filteredCommitments.length > 0 ? (
269 |                 <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
270 |                   {filteredCommitments.map((commitment) => (
271 |                     <CommitmentCard key={commitment.id} {...commitment} />
272 |                   ))}
273 |                 </div>
274 |               ) : (
275 |                 <div className="text-center py-12 bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-lg border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 shadow-md">
276 |                   <Filter className="h-12 w-12 mx-auto text-gray-400 mb-4" />
277 |                   <p className="text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 text-lg font-medium mb-2">No commitments found</p>
278 |                   <p className="text-gray-400 dark:text-gray-500 mb-6">Try adjusting your search or filters</p>
279 |                   <Link to="/create-commitment">
280 |                     <Button className="bg-connect-500 hover:bg-connect-600">
281 |                       <PlusCircle className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
282 |                       Create New Commitment
283 |                     </Button>
284 |                   </Link>
285 |                 </div>
286 |               )}
287 |             </TabsContent>
288 |             
289 |             <TabsContent value="active" className="mt-0">
290 |               {activeCommitments.length > 0 ? (
291 |                 <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
292 |                   {activeCommitments.map((commitment) => (
293 |                     <CommitmentCard key={commitment.id} {...commitment} />
294 |                   ))}
295 |                 </div>
296 |               ) : (
297 |                 <div className="text-center py-12 bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-lg border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 shadow-md">
298 |                   <p className="text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">No active commitments found.</p>
299 |                 </div>
300 |               )}
301 |             </TabsContent>
302 |             
303 |             <TabsContent value="pending" className="mt-0">
304 |               {pendingCommitments.length > 0 ? (
305 |                 <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
306 |                   {pendingCommitments.map((commitment) => (
307 |                     <CommitmentCard key={commitment.id} {...commitment} />
308 |                   ))}
309 |                 </div>
310 |               ) : (
311 |                 <div className="text-center py-12 bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-lg border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 shadow-md">
312 |                   <p className="text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">No pending commitments found.</p>
313 |                 </div>
314 |               )}
315 |             </TabsContent>
316 |             
317 |             <TabsContent value="completed" className="mt-0">
318 |               {completedCommitments.length > 0 ? (
319 |                 <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
320 |                   {completedCommitments.map((commitment) => (
321 |                     <CommitmentCard key={commitment.id} {...commitment} />
322 |                   ))}
323 |                 </div>
324 |               ) : (
325 |                 <div className="text-center py-12 bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-lg border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 shadow-md">
326 |                   <p className="text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">No completed commitments found.</p>
327 |                 </div>
328 |               )}
329 |             </TabsContent>
330 |           </Tabs>
331 |         </div>
332 |       </main>
333 |       
334 |       <Footer />
335 |     </div>
336 |   );
337 | };

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/src/services/CommitmentService.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1 | 
  2 | import { supabase } from "@/integrations/supabase/client";
  3 | import { Commitment, CommitmentStatus, CommitmentType } from "@/types/commitments";
  4 | 
  5 | export class CommitmentService {
  6 |   /**
  7 |    * Creates a new commitment
  8 |    * @param commitment Commitment data to create
  9 |    * @returns The created commitment with its id
 10 |    */
 11 |   static async createCommitment(commitment: Omit<Commitment, 'id'>): Promise<Commitment> {
 12 |     // Map the commitment data to match the database schema
 13 |     const commitmentData = {
 14 |       title: commitment.title,
 15 |       description: commitment.description,
 16 |       type: commitment.type,
 17 |       status: commitment.status,
 18 |       created_by: commitment.createdBy,
 19 |       deadline: commitment.deadline,
 20 |       value: commitment.value,
 21 |       
 22 |       // Type-specific fields
 23 |       is_public: 'isPublic' in commitment ? (commitment as any).isPublic : null,
 24 |       goal: 'goal' in commitment ? (commitment as any).goal : null,
 25 |       milestone: 'milestone' in commitment ? (commitment as any).milestone : null,
 26 |       terms: 'terms' in commitment ? (commitment as any).terms : null,
 27 |       contract_type: 'contractType' in commitment ? (commitment as any).contractType : null,
 28 |       contract_details: 'contractDetails' in commitment ? (commitment as any).contractDetails : null,
 29 |       religion: 'religion' in commitment ? (commitment as any).religion : null,
 30 |       deity: 'deity' in commitment ? (commitment as any).deity : null,
 31 |       ritual: 'ritual' in commitment ? (commitment as any).ritual : null,
 32 |       promise_type: 'promiseType' in commitment ? (commitment as any).promiseType : null,
 33 |       occasion: 'occasion' in commitment ? (commitment as any).occasion : null,
 34 |       secret_encrypted: 'secretEncrypted' in commitment ? (commitment as any).secretEncrypted : null,
 35 |       trust_level: 'trustLevel' in commitment ? (commitment as any).trustLevel : null
 36 |     };
 37 |     
 38 |     // Insert the commitment
 39 |     const { data, error } = await supabase
 40 |       .from('commitments')
 41 |       .insert(commitmentData)
 42 |       .select()
 43 |       .single();
 44 |     
 45 |     if (error) {
 46 |       console.error("Error creating commitment:", error);
 47 |       throw new Error(`Failed to create commitment: ${error.message}`);
 48 |     }
 49 |     
 50 |     // Then, if there are parties, insert them
 51 |     if (commitment.parties && commitment.parties.length > 0) {
 52 |       const partiesData = commitment.parties.map(party => ({
 53 |         commitment_id: data.id,
 54 |         user_id: party.id,
 55 |         name: party.name,
 56 |         email: party.email || null,
 57 |         role: party.role
 58 |       }));
 59 |       
 60 |       const { error: partiesError } = await supabase
 61 |         .from('commitment_parties')
 62 |         .insert(partiesData);
 63 |         
 64 |       if (partiesError) {
 65 |         console.error("Error adding commitment parties:", partiesError);
 66 |         // We don't throw here to avoid transaction-like behavior that's hard to handle
 67 |         // The commitment is created, but parties might not be
 68 |       }
 69 |     }
 70 |     
 71 |     // Map the DB response back to our app's Commitment type
 72 |     return mapDbCommitmentToAppCommitment(data);
 73 |   }
 74 |   
 75 |   /**
 76 |    * Gets all commitments for the current user
 77 |    * @returns List of commitments
 78 |    */
 79 |   static async getUserCommitments(): Promise<Commitment[]> {
 80 |     const { data: user } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
 81 |     
 82 |     if (!user.user) {
 83 |       throw new Error("User not authenticated");
 84 |     }
 85 |     
 86 |     const { data, error } = await supabase
 87 |       .from('commitments')
 88 |       .select(`
 89 |         *,
 90 |         commitment_parties(*)
 91 |       `)
 92 |       .eq('created_by', user.user.id)
 93 |       .order('created_at', { ascending: false });
 94 |       
 95 |     if (error) {
 96 |       console.error("Error fetching commitments:", error);
 97 |       throw new Error(`Failed to fetch commitments: ${error.message}`);
 98 |     }
 99 |     
100 |     return data.map(mapDbCommitmentToAppCommitment);
101 |   }
102 |   
103 |   /**
104 |    * Gets commitments where the user is a participant
105 |    * @returns List of commitments
106 |    */
107 |   static async getParticipatingCommitments(): Promise<Commitment[]> {
108 |     const { data: user } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
109 |     
110 |     if (!user.user) {
111 |       throw new Error("User not authenticated");
112 |     }
113 |     
114 |     // First get all commitment IDs where the user is a party
115 |     const { data: partyData, error: partyError } = await supabase
116 |       .from('commitment_parties')
117 |       .select('commitment_id')
118 |       .eq('user_id', user.user.id);
119 |       
120 |     if (partyError) {
121 |       console.error("Error fetching participating commitments:", partyError);
122 |       throw new Error(`Failed to fetch participating commitments: ${partyError.message}`);
123 |     }
124 |     
125 |     if (!partyData || partyData.length === 0) {
126 |       return [];
127 |     }
128 |     
129 |     // Then get the actual commitments
130 |     const commitmentIds = partyData.map(item => item.commitment_id);
131 |     
132 |     const { data, error } = await supabase
133 |       .from('commitments')
134 |       .select(`
135 |         *,
136 |         commitment_parties(*)
137 |       `)
138 |       .in('id', commitmentIds)
139 |       .order('created_at', { ascending: false });
140 |       
141 |     if (error) {
142 |       console.error("Error fetching commitments by IDs:", error);
143 |       throw new Error(`Failed to fetch commitments by IDs: ${error.message}`);
144 |     }
145 |     
146 |     return data.map(mapDbCommitmentToAppCommitment);
147 |   }
148 |   
149 |   /**
150 |    * Gets a commitment by its ID
151 |    * @param id The commitment ID
152 |    * @returns The commitment or null if not found
153 |    */
154 |   static async getCommitmentById(id: string): Promise<Commitment | null> {
155 |     const { data, error } = await supabase
156 |       .from('commitments')
157 |       .select(`
158 |         *,
159 |         commitment_parties(*)
160 |       `)
161 |       .eq('id', id)
162 |       .maybeSingle();
163 |       
164 |     if (error) {
165 |       console.error("Error fetching commitment:", error);
166 |       throw new Error(`Failed to fetch commitment: ${error.message}`);
167 |     }
168 |     
169 |     if (!data) return null;
170 |     
171 |     return mapDbCommitmentToAppCommitment(data);
172 |   }
173 |   
174 |   /**
175 |    * Updates a commitment by its ID
176 |    * @param id The commitment ID
177 |    * @param updates The fields to update
178 |    * @returns The updated commitment
179 |    */
180 |   static async updateCommitment(id: string, updates: Partial<Commitment>): Promise<Commitment> {
181 |     // Map the updates to match the database schema
182 |     const dbUpdates: any = {};
183 |     
184 |     if (updates.title) dbUpdates.title = updates.title;
185 |     if (updates.description) dbUpdates.description = updates.description;
186 |     if (updates.status) dbUpdates.status = updates.status;
187 |     if (updates.deadline) dbUpdates.deadline = updates.deadline;
188 |     if (updates.value !== undefined) dbUpdates.value = updates.value;
189 |     
190 |     // Handle type-specific fields
191 |     if ('isPublic' in updates) dbUpdates.is_public = (updates as any).isPublic;
192 |     if ('goal' in updates) dbUpdates.goal = (updates as any).goal;
193 |     if ('milestone' in updates) dbUpdates.milestone = (updates as any).milestone;
194 |     if ('terms' in updates) dbUpdates.terms = (updates as any).terms;
195 |     if ('contractType' in updates) dbUpdates.contract_type = (updates as any).contractType;
196 |     if ('contractDetails' in updates) dbUpdates.contract_details = (updates as any).contractDetails;
197 |     if ('religion' in updates) dbUpdates.religion = (updates as any).religion;
198 |     if ('deity' in updates) dbUpdates.deity = (updates as any).deity;
199 |     if ('ritual' in updates) dbUpdates.ritual = (updates as any).ritual;
200 |     if ('promiseType' in updates) dbUpdates.promise_type = (updates as any).promiseType;
201 |     if ('occasion' in updates) dbUpdates.occasion = (updates as any).occasion;
202 |     if ('secretEncrypted' in updates) dbUpdates.secret_encrypted = (updates as any).secretEncrypted;
203 |     if ('trustLevel' in updates) dbUpdates.trust_level = (updates as any).trustLevel;
204 | 
205 |     // Add updated_at timestamp
206 |     dbUpdates.updated_at = new Date().toISOString();
207 |     
208 |     const { data, error } = await supabase
209 |       .from('commitments')
210 |       .update(dbUpdates)
211 |       .eq('id', id)
212 |       .select(`
213 |         *,
214 |         commitment_parties(*)
215 |       `)
216 |       .single();
217 |       
218 |     if (error) {
219 |       console.error("Error updating commitment:", error);
220 |       throw new Error(`Failed to update commitment: ${error.message}`);
221 |     }
222 |     
223 |     // Update parties if provided
224 |     if (updates.parties) {
225 |       // First, delete existing parties
226 |       const { error: deleteError } = await supabase
227 |         .from('commitment_parties')
228 |         .delete()
229 |         .eq('commitment_id', id);
230 |         
231 |       if (deleteError) {
232 |         console.error("Error deleting existing parties:", deleteError);
233 |         // Continue anyway to try inserting new parties
234 |       }
235 |       
236 |       // Then insert new parties
237 |       const partiesData = updates.parties.map(party => ({
238 |         commitment_id: id,
239 |         user_id: party.id,
240 |         name: party.name,
241 |         email: party.email || null,
242 |         role: party.role
243 |       }));
244 |       
245 |       if (partiesData.length > 0) {
246 |         const { error: insertError } = await supabase
247 |           .from('commitment_parties')
248 |           .insert(partiesData);
249 |           
250 |         if (insertError) {
251 |           console.error("Error inserting new parties:", insertError);
252 |           // Continue anyway, commitment is updated
253 |         }
254 |       }
255 |     }
256 |     
257 |     return mapDbCommitmentToAppCommitment(data);
258 |   }
259 |   
260 |   /**
261 |    * Updates the status of a commitment
262 |    * @param id The commitment ID
263 |    * @param status The new status
264 |    * @returns The updated commitment
265 |    */
266 |   static async updateCommitmentStatus(id: string, status: CommitmentStatus): Promise<Commitment> {
267 |     return this.updateCommitment(id, { status });
268 |   }
269 |   
270 |   /**
271 |    * Deletes a commitment by its ID
272 |    * @param id The commitment ID
273 |    */
274 |   static async deleteCommitment(id: string): Promise<void> {
275 |     const { error } = await supabase
276 |       .from('commitments')
277 |       .delete()
278 |       .eq('id', id);
279 |       
280 |     if (error) {
281 |       console.error("Error deleting commitment:", error);
282 |       throw new Error(`Failed to delete commitment: ${error.message}`);
283 |     }
284 |   }
285 |   
286 |   /**
287 |    * Gets all commitment types from the database
288 |    * @returns List of commitment types
289 |    */
290 |   static async getCommitmentTypes(): Promise<CommitmentType[]> {
291 |     const { data, error } = await supabase
292 |       .from('commitment_types')
293 |       .select('name');
294 |       
295 |     if (error) {
296 |       console.error("Error fetching commitment types:", error);
297 |       throw new Error(`Failed to fetch commitment types: ${error.message}`);
298 |     }
299 |     
300 |     return data.map(type => type.name as CommitmentType);
301 |   }
302 | }
303 | 
304 | /**
305 |  * Helper function to map database commitment objects to application commitment objects
306 |  */
307 | function mapDbCommitmentToAppCommitment(dbCommitment: any): Commitment {
308 |   // Map parties if they exist
309 |   const parties = dbCommitment.commitment_parties 
310 |     ? dbCommitment.commitment_parties.map((party: any) => ({
311 |         id: party.user_id,
312 |         name: party.name,
313 |         email: party.email || undefined,
314 |         role: party.role as "associated" | "informed"
315 |       }))
316 |     : [];
317 | 
318 |   // Create base commitment
319 |   const baseCommitment = {
320 |     id: dbCommitment.id,
321 |     title: dbCommitment.title,
322 |     description: dbCommitment.description,
323 |     type: dbCommitment.type as CommitmentType,
324 |     createdAt: dbCommitment.created_at,
325 |     deadline: dbCommitment.deadline || undefined,
326 |     status: dbCommitment.status as CommitmentStatus,
327 |     createdBy: dbCommitment.created_by,
328 |     parties: parties,
329 |     value: dbCommitment.value || undefined
330 |   };
331 |   
332 |   // Add type-specific fields
333 |   switch (dbCommitment.type) {
334 |     case 'personal':
335 |       return {
336 |         ...baseCommitment,
337 |         type: 'personal',
338 |         isPublic: !!dbCommitment.is_public,
339 |         goal: dbCommitment.goal || '',
340 |         milestone: dbCommitment.milestone
341 |       };
342 |       
343 |     case 'business':
344 |       return {
345 |         ...baseCommitment,
346 |         type: 'business',
347 |         documents: [], // We would need to fetch these separately if needed
348 |         terms: dbCommitment.terms
349 |       };
350 |       
351 |     case 'contract':
352 |       return {
353 |         ...baseCommitment,
354 |         type: 'contract',
355 |         contractType: dbCommitment.contract_type as any || 'other',
356 |         contractDetails: dbCommitment.contract_details || '',
357 |         documents: [] // We would need to fetch these separately if needed
358 |       };
359 |       
360 |     case 'religious':
361 |       return {
362 |         ...baseCommitment,
363 |         type: 'religious',
364 |         religion: dbCommitment.religion || '',
365 |         deity: dbCommitment.deity || '',
366 |         ritual: dbCommitment.ritual
367 |       };
368 |       
369 |     case 'promise':
370 |       return {
371 |         ...baseCommitment,
372 |         type: 'promise',
373 |         promiseType: dbCommitment.promise_type || ''
374 |       };
375 |       
376 |     case 'friendly':
377 |       return {
378 |         ...baseCommitment,
379 |         type: 'friendly',
380 |         occasion: dbCommitment.occasion
381 |       };
382 |       
383 |     case 'trust':
384 |       return {
385 |         ...baseCommitment,
386 |         type: 'trust',
387 |         secretEncrypted: dbCommitment.secret_encrypted || '',
388 |         trustLevel: (dbCommitment.trust_level as any) || 'medium'
389 |       };
390 |       
391 |     default:
392 |       // Fallback to basic commitment type
393 |       return {
394 |         ...baseCommitment,
395 |         type: dbCommitment.type as CommitmentType
396 |       } as Commitment;
397 |   }
398 | }
399 |

 1 | 
 2 | export type CommitmentStatus = "active" | "pending" | "completed" | "expired";
 3 | 
 4 | export type CommitmentType = 
 5 |   | "personal" 
 6 |   | "business" 
 7 |   | "contract" 
 8 |   | "religious" 
 9 |   | "promise"
10 |   | "friendly"
11 |   | "trust";
12 | 
13 | export interface TaggedUser {
14 |   id: string;
15 |   name: string;
16 |   email?: string;
17 |   role: "associated" | "informed";
18 | }
19 | 
20 | export interface BaseCommitment {
21 |   id?: string;
22 |   title: string;
23 |   description: string;
24 |   type: CommitmentType;
25 |   createdAt: string;
26 |   deadline?: string;
27 |   status: CommitmentStatus;
28 |   createdBy: string;
29 |   parties: TaggedUser[];
30 |   value?: number;
31 | }
32 | 
33 | export interface PersonalCommitment extends BaseCommitment {
34 |   type: "personal";
35 |   isPublic: boolean;
36 |   goal: string;
37 |   milestone?: string;
38 | }
39 | 
40 | export interface BusinessCommitment extends BaseCommitment {
41 |   type: "business";
42 |   documents: {
43 |     name: string;
44 |     url: string;
45 |     type: "contract" | "invoice" | "receipt" | "negotiation" | "other";
46 |     uploadedAt: string;
47 |   }[];
48 |   terms?: string;
49 | }
50 | 
51 | export interface ContractCommitment extends BaseCommitment {
52 |   type: "contract";
53 |   contractType: "sponsorship" | "employment" | "service" | "termsheet" | "other";
54 |   contractDetails: string;
55 |   documents: {
56 |     name: string;
57 |     url: string;
58 |     uploadedAt: string;
59 |   }[];
60 | }
61 | 
62 | export interface ReligiousCommitment extends BaseCommitment {
63 |   type: "religious";
64 |   religion: string;
65 |   deity: string;
66 |   ritual?: string;
67 | }
68 | 
69 | export interface PromiseCommitment extends BaseCommitment {
70 |   type: "promise";
71 |   promiseType: string;
72 | }
73 | 
74 | export interface FriendlyCommitment extends BaseCommitment {
75 |   type: "friendly";
76 |   occasion?: string;
77 | }
78 | 
79 | export interface TrustCommitment extends BaseCommitment {
80 |   type: "trust";
81 |   secretEncrypted: string;
82 |   trustLevel: "low" | "medium" | "high";
83 | }
84 | 
85 | export type Commitment = 
86 |   | PersonalCommitment 
87 |   | BusinessCommitment 
88 |   | ContractCommitment 
89 |   | ReligiousCommitment 
90 |   | PromiseCommitment
91 |   | FriendlyCommitment
92 |   | TrustCommitment;
